  🤖 AI_ANSWER  ~274 tok
    Я вижу следующие таблицы в базе данных ClickHouse:  1.
    **dm_campaign_funnel** - воронка кампаний (utm_source, utm_campaign, visits,
    new_users, bounces и др.) 2. **dm_client_journey** - путешествия клиентов
    (client_id, date, utm_source, device, has_purchase и др.) 3.
    **dm_client_profile** - профили клиентов (client_id, first_visit_date,
    total_visits, has_purchased и др.) 4. **dm_conversion_paths** - пути
    конверсии (client_id, converted, revenue, channels_path и др.) 5.
    **dm_orders** - заказы (order_id, client_id, order_revenue, utm_source,
    days_to_purchase и др.) 6. **dm_products** - товары (product_id,
    product_name, product_category, total_revenue и др.) 7. **dm_purchases** -
    покупки (client_id, product_id, product_name, quantity, estimated_revenue и
    др.) 8. **dm_traffic_performance** - производительность трафика (date,
    utm_source, device, visits, revenue и др.) 9. **visits** - визиты (visitID,
    date, clientID, deviceCategory, UTMSource, purchaseRevenue и др.)  Это
    полный набор витрин для анализа маркетинговых данных. Схема каждой таблицы с
    типами полей уже загружена в моей памяти.

      SELECT 
          'utm_source' AS field,
          'Источник трафика (UTM source)' AS description,
          arrayDistinct(arraySlice(arraySort(groupArray(utm_source)), 1, 3)) AS example_values,
          uniq(utm_source) AS unique_count,
          countIf(utm_source = '') AS empty_count,
          countIf(utm_source != '') AS non_empty_count
      FROM dm_campaign_funnel
      WHERE utm_source != ''
      GROUP BY 1, 2
      
      UNION ALL
      
      SELECT 
          'utm_campaign' AS field,
          'Название кампании (UTM campaign)' AS description,
          arrayDistinct(arraySlice(arraySort(groupArray(utm_campaign)), 1, 3)) AS example_values,
          uniq(utm_campaign) AS unique_count,
          countIf(utm_campaign = '') AS empty_count,
          countIf(utm_campaign != '') AS non_empty_count
      FROM dm_campaign_funnel
      WHERE utm_campaign != ''
      GROUP BY 1, 2
      
      UNION ALL
      
      SELECT 
          'visits' AS field,
          'Всего визитов (включая анонимные)' AS description,

      import numpy as np

      # Получаем примеры непустых значений для каждого поля
      df = df.copy()
      
      # Определяем структуру описания
      fields_info = {
          'utm_source': {
              'description': 'Источник трафика (UTM source)',
              'type': 'String',
              'examples': df['utm_source'].dropna().unique()[:3].tolist()
          },
          'utm_campaign': {
              'description': 'Название кампании (UTM campaign)',
              'type': 'String',
              'examples': df['utm_campaign'].dropna().unique()[:3].tolist()
          },
          'visits': {
              'description': 'Всего визитов (включая анонимные сессии с clientID = 0)',
              'type': 'UInt64',
              'examples': sorted(df['visits'].dropna().unique())[:3]
          },
          'new_users': {
              'description': 'Новых пользователей (первый визит с данного источника/кампании)',
              'type': 'UInt64',
              'examples': sorted(df['new_users'].dropna().unique())[:3]
          },
          'bounces': {
              'description': 'Отказов (одностраничных сессий)',
              'type': 'UInt64',
              'examples': sorted(df['bounces'].dropna().unique())[:3]
          },
          'total_duration': {
              'description': 'Общая длительность всех визитов в секундах',
              'type': 'UInt64',
              'examples': sorted(df['total_duration'].dropna().unique())[:3]
          },
          'total_pageviews': {
              'description': 'Общее количество просмотров страниц во всех визитах',
              'type': 'UInt64',
              'examples': sorted(df['total_pageviews'].dropna().unique())[:3]
          },
          'sessions_with_purchase': {
              'description': 'Сессий, в которых была совершена покупка',
              'type': 'UInt64',
              'examples': sorted(df['sessions_with_purchase'].dropna().unique())[:3]
          },
          'revenue': {
              'description': 'Выручка от кампании (сумма всех покупок)',
              'type': 'Float64',
              'examples': sorted(df['revenue'].dropna().unique())[:3]
          },
          'pre_purchase_visits': {
              'description': 'Визитов до покупки (pre-purchase visits)',
              'type': 'UInt64',
              'examples': sorted(df['pre_purchase_visits'].dropna().unique())[:3]
          },
          'unique_clients_pre_purchase': {
              'description': 'Уникальных клиентов, совершивших визиты до покупки',
              'type': 'UInt64',
              'examples': sorted(df['unique_clients_pre_purchase'].dropna().unique())[:3]
          },
          'unique_buyers': {
              'description': 'Уникальных покупателей (клиентов, совершивших покупку)',
              'type': 'UInt64',
              'examples': sorted(df['unique_buyers'].dropna().unique())[:3]
          }
      }
      
      # Формируем вывод
      result = "## Таблица dm_campaign_funnel: Воронка кампаний\n\n"
      result += "**Назначение**: Агрегированные метрики эффективности по комбинациям UTM source + UTM campaign\n\n"
      
      result += "| Поле | Тип | Описание | Примеры значений |\n"
      result += "|------|-----|----------|------------------|\n"
      
      for field_name, info in fields_info.items():
          examples = info['examples']
          if isinstance(examples[0], (int, float)):
              examples_str = ', '.join([str(x) for x in examples])
          else:
              examples_str = ', '.join([f'"{x}"' for x in examples])
          
          result += f"| {field_name} | {info['type']} | {info['description']} | {examples_str} |\n"
      
      result += "\n"
      
      # Добавляем ключевые метрики воронки
      result += "### Ключевые показатели:\n"
      result += "1. **CR (Conversion Rate)** = sessions_with_purchase / visits × 100%\n"
      result += "2. **Bounce Rate** = bounces / visits × 100%\n"
      result += "3. **Avg. Session Duration** = total_duration / visits (сек)\n"
      result += "4. **Avg. Pageviews per Visit** = total_pageviews / visits\n"
      result += "5. **New User Rate** = new_users / visits × 100%\n"
      result += "6. **Revenue per Visit** = revenue / visits\n\n"
      
      result += "### Особенности данных:\n"
      result += "• **visits** включает все визиты (включая анонимные с clientID = 0)\n"
      result += "• **unique_buyers** считает только клиентов с clientID > 0\n"
      result += "• Метрики pre_purchase показывают взаимодействия до конверсии\n"
      
      print(result)

      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      
      print("Первые 5 строк dm_campaign_funnel:")
      print(df.to_string(index=False))
      
      print("\n" + "="*80)
      print("Краткая статистика по числовым полям:")
      
      # Форматирование чисел с разделителями
      def fmt_num(x):
          if pd.isna(x):
              return "—"
          if isinstance(x, (int, np.integer)):
              return f"{x:,}".replace(",", " ")
          if isinstance(x, (float, np.floating)):
              return f"{x:,.0f}".replace(",", " ")
          return str(x)
      
      num_cols = df.select_dtypes(include=[np.number]).columns
      for col in num_cols:
          print(f"\n{col}:")
          print(f"  Минимум: {fmt_num(df[col].min())}")
          print(f"  Максимум: {fmt_num(df[col].max())}")
          print(f"  Сумма: {fmt_num(df[col].sum())}")

      SELECT 
          product_name,
          product_category,
          count() AS orders,
          sum(quantity) AS qty,
          round(sum(estimated_revenue)) AS revenue,
          round(avg(unit_price)) AS avg_unit_price
      FROM dm_purchases
      GROUP BY product_name, product_category
      ORDER BY orders DESC
      LIMIT 30

      SELECT 
          utm_source_last AS utm_source,
          count() AS orders,
          round(avg(order_revenue)) AS avg_check,
          round(sum(order_revenue)) AS total_revenue
      FROM dm_orders
      GROUP BY utm_source_last
      ORDER BY orders DESC
      LIMIT 20

    SQL:
      
      -- Топ товаров: все источники
      WITH orders_src AS (
          SELECT order_id, utm_source_last AS utm_source, order_revenue
          FROM dm_orders
      )
      SELECT 
          p.product_name,
          p.product_category,
          count(DISTINCT p.order_id) AS orders,
          sum(p.quantity) AS qty,
          round(avg(o.order_revenue)) AS avg_order_check,
          round(avg(p.unit_price)) AS avg_unit_price,
          -- доля Директа
          countIf(DISTINCT p.order_id, o.utm_source = 'yandex') AS orders_yandex,
          countIf(DISTINCT p.order_id, o.utm_source != 'yandex') AS orders_other
      FROM dm_purchases p
      LEFT JOIN orders_src o ON p.order_id = o.order_id
      GROUP BY p.product_name, p.product_category
      ORDER BY orders DESC
      LIMIT 25

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [clickhouse_query]  ~73 tok

      -- Средний чек по источникам (для контекста)

          round(sum(order_revenue)) AS total_revenue
      FROM dm_orders
      GROUP BY utm_source_last
      ORDER BY orders DESC
      LIMIT 15

    CODE:
      
      df_products = pd.read_parquet("/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_60cdca4366.parquet")
      df_sources = pd.read_parquet("/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_8c8d7a6802.parquet")
      
      # --- Топ товаров ---
      df_products['revenue'] = pd.to_numeric(df_products['revenue'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)
      df_products['orders'] = pd.to_numeric(df_products['orders'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)
      df_products['qty'] = pd.to_numeric(df_products['qty'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)
      
      # Укорачиваем длинные названия
      def short(name, n=55):
          return name if len(str(name)) <= n else str(name)[:n] + '…'
      
      df_products['short_name'] = df_products['product_name'].apply(lambda x: short(x))
      
      # Таблица топ-15
      top15 = df_products.head(15)
      
      lines = ["## Топ-15 товаров по числу заказов\n"]
      lines.append("| # | Товар | Категория | Заказов | Кол-во | Выручка |")
      lines.append("|---|---|---|---:|---:|---:|")
      for i, row in top15.iterrows():
          lines.append(f"| {i+1} | {short(row['product_name'], 50)} | {row['product_category']} | {int(row['orders']):,} | {int(row['qty']):,} | {row['revenue']:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      # --- Средний чек по источникам ---
      lines.append("\n## Средний чек по источникам трафика\n")
      lines.append("| Источник | Заказов | Средний чек | Выручка |")
      lines.append("|---|---:|---:|---:|")
      
      source_labels = {
          '': 'Прямой / не размечен',
          'ya-direct': 'Яндекс.Директ',
          'gdeslon': 'Gdeslon (CPA)',
          'yandexsmartcamera': 'Яндекс Smart Camera',
          'cityads': 'CityAds (CPA)',
      }
      
      for _, row in df_sources.iterrows():
          label = source_labels.get(row['utm_source_last'], row['utm_source_last'])
          lines.append(f"| {label} | {int(row['orders']):,} | {int(row['avg_check']):,} ₽ | {row['total_revenue']:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      result = "\n".join(lines)
      print(result)

    CODE:
      
      df_products = pd.read_parquet("/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_60cdca4366.parquet")
      df_sources = pd.read_parquet("/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_8c8d7a6802.parquet")
      
      df_products['revenue'] = pd.to_numeric(df_products['revenue'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)
      df_products['orders'] = pd.to_numeric(df_products['orders'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)
      df_products['qty'] = pd.to_numeric(df_products['qty'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)
      df_sources['orders'] = pd.to_numeric(df_sources['orders'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)
      df_sources['avg_check'] = pd.to_numeric(df_sources['avg_check'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)
      df_sources['total_revenue'] = pd.to_numeric(df_sources['total_revenue'], errors='coerce').fillna(0)
      
      top15 = df_products.head(15).reset_index(drop=True)
      
      lines = ["## Топ-15 товаров по числу заказов\n"]
      lines.append("| # | Товар | Категория | Заказов | Кол-во | Выручка |")
      lines.append("|---|---|---|---:|---:|---:|")
      for i, row in top15.iterrows():
          name = str(row['product_name'])
          if len(name) > 50:
              name = name[:50] + '…'
          cat = str(row['product_category'])
          lines.append(f"| {i+1} | {name} | {cat} | {int(row['orders']):,} | {int(row['qty']):,} | {row['revenue']:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      lines.append("\n## Средний чек по источникам трафика\n")
      lines.append("| Источник | Заказов | Средний чек | Выручка |")
      lines.append("|---|---:|---:|---:|")
      
      source_labels = {
          '': 'Прямой / не размечен',
          'ya-direct': 'Яндекс.Директ',
          'gdeslon': 'Gdeslon (CPA)',
          'yandexsmartcamera': 'Яндекс Smart Camera',
          'cityads': 'CityAds (CPA)',
      }
      
      for _, row in df_sources.iterrows():
          src = str(row['utm_source_last']) if pd.notna(row['utm_source_last']) else ''
          label = source_labels.get(src, src)
          lines.append(f"| {label} | {int(row['orders']):,} | {int(row['avg_check']):,} ₽ | {row['total_revenue']:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      result = "\n".join(lines)
      print(result)

    товаров** из `dm_purchases` — по числу заказов, количеству и выручке
    (`product_name`, `product_category`, `orders`, `qty`, `revenue`).  **Средний
    чек по источникам** из `dm_orders` — 5 строк: источники, число заказов,

    отформатировать — Python упал на `NameError` в первой попытке, вторая не
    вернула `result` до исчерпания лимита.  ---  ## Что не успел  - Показать
    тебе читаемые таблицы с данными - Сравнить товарный микс Директа vs других
    источников (нужен отдельный запрос с `GROUP BY product_name,
    utm_source_last`)  ---  ## Что исследовать дальше  Задай заново — данные уже
    известны, запросы рабочие, в следующей сессии сразу получишь результат:  1.
    **"Покажи топ товаров"** — выдам таблицу топ-15 с заказами, штуками и

      SELECT 
          product_name,
          COUNT() AS orders_count,
          SUM(quantity) AS total_quantity,
          ROUND(SUM(product_revenue), 2) AS total_revenue,
          COUNT(DISTINCT client_id) AS unique_clients,
          ROUND(AVG(product_revenue), 2) AS avg_product_value
      FROM dm_purchases
      WHERE product_name != ''
      GROUP BY product_name
      ORDER BY orders_count DESC
      LIMIT 20

      df_display['total_revenue'] = df_display['total_revenue'].round(2)

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [clickhouse_query]  ~313 tok
    SQL:
      WITH товары_директ AS (
          SELECT 
              product_name,
              COUNT() AS orders_count_direct,
              SUM(quantity) AS total_quantity_direct,
              ROUND(SUM(product_revenue), 2) AS total_revenue_direct,
              ROUND(AVG(product_revenue), 2) AS avg_price_direct
          FROM dm_purchases
          WHERE product_name != '' AND utm_source = 'yandex_direct'
          GROUP BY product_name
      ),
      товары_другие AS (
          SELECT 
              product_name,
              COUNT() AS orders_count_other,
              SUM(quantity) AS total_quantity_other,
              ROUND(SUM(product_revenue), 2) AS total_revenue_other,
              ROUND(AVG(product_revenue), 2) AS avg_price_other
          FROM dm_purchases
          WHERE product_name != '' AND utm_source != 'yandex_direct' AND utm_source != ''
          GROUP BY product_name
      )
      SELECT 
          COALESCE(д.продукт, д.продукт) AS product_name,
          д.orders_count_direct,
          д.total_revenue_direct,
          д.avg_price_direct,
          о.orders_count_other,
          о.total_revenue_other,
          о.avg_price_other
      FROM товары_директ д
      FULL OUTER JOIN товары_другие о ON д.product_name = о.product_name
      WHERE (д.orders_count_direct > 0 OR о.orders_count_other > 0)
      ORDER BY (д.orders_count_direct + о.orders_count_other) DESC
      LIMIT 30

      WITH товары_директ AS (
          SELECT 
              product_name,
              COUNT() AS orders_count_direct,
              SUM(quantity) AS total_quantity_direct,
              ROUND(SUM(product_revenue), 2) AS total_revenue_direct,
              ROUND(AVG(product_revenue), 2) AS avg_price_direct
          FROM dm_purchases
          WHERE product_name != '' AND utm_source = 'yandex_direct'
          GROUP BY product_name
      ),
      товары_другие AS (
          SELECT 
              product_name,
              COUNT() AS orders_count_other,
              SUM(quantity) AS total_quantity_other,
              ROUND(SUM(product_revenue), 2) AS total_revenue_other,
              ROUND(AVG(product_revenue), 2) AS avg_price_other
          FROM dm_purchases
          WHERE product_name != '' AND utm_source != 'yandex_direct' AND utm_source != ''
          GROUP BY product_name
      )
      SELECT 
          COALESCE(д.product_name, о.product_name) AS product_name,
          COALESCE(д.orders_count_direct, 0) AS orders_count_direct,
          COALESCE(д.total_revenue_direct, 0) AS total_revenue_direct,
          COALESCE(д.avg_price_direct, 0) AS avg_price_direct,
          COALESCE(о.orders_count_other, 0) AS orders_count_other,
          COALESCE(о.total_revenue_other, 0) AS total_revenue_other,
          COALESCE(о.avg_price_other, 0) AS avg_price_other
      FROM товары_директ д
      FULL OUTER JOIN товары_другие о ON д.product_name = о.product_name
      WHERE (COALESCE(д.orders_count_direct, 0) > 0 OR COALESCE(о.orders_count_other, 0) > 0)
      ORDER BY (COALESCE(д.orders_count_direct, 0) + COALESCE(о.orders_count_other, 0)) DESC
      LIMIT 30

    CODE:
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      
      print("📊 Сравнение товаров по источникам трафика")
      
      # Создаем DataFrame из данных
      df_combined = df.copy()
      
      # Группируем по товару для сравнения
      df_pivot = df_combined.pivot_table(
          index='product_name',
          columns='utm_source',
          values=['orders_count', 'total_revenue'],
          aggfunc='sum',
          fill_value=0
      )
      
      # Упрощаем структуру
      df_comp = pd.DataFrame()
      for source in df_combined['utm_source'].unique():
          orders_col = ('orders_count', source)
          revenue_col = ('total_revenue', source)
          if orders_col in df_pivot.columns:
              df_comp[f'orders_{source}'] = df_pivot[orders_col]
              df_comp[f'revenue_{source}'] = df_pivot[revenue_col]
      
      # Сортируем по суммарным заказам
      df_comp['total_orders'] = df_comp.sum(axis=1)
      df_comp = df_comp.sort_values('total_orders', ascending=False).head(15)
      
      # Форматируем для вывода
      def shorten_name(name, max_len=60):
          if isinstance(name, str) and len(name) > max_len:
              return name[:max_len-3] + "..."
          return name
      
      df_comp['product_short'] = df_comp.index.map(lambda x: shorten_name(x, 60))
      
      result = "## Часть 2: Сравнение товаров по источникам трафика\n\n"
      result += "**Топ товаров по источникам:**\n"
      result += "| Товар | Заказов (Директ) | Выручка (Директ) | Заказов (Другие) | Выручка (Другие) |\n"
      result += "|---|---|---|---|---|\n"
      
      for idx, row in df_comp.iterrows():
          orders_direct = int(row.get('orders_ya-direct', 0))
          revenue_direct = float(row.get('revenue_ya-direct', 0))
          orders_other = int(row.get('orders_gdeslon', 0))
          revenue_other = float(row.get('revenue_gdeslon', 0))
          
          result += f"| {row['product_short']} | {orders_direct:,} | {revenue_direct:,.0f} ₽ | {orders_other:,} | {revenue_other:,.0f} ₽ |\n"
      
      # Общая статистика по источникам
      total_orders_direct = df_combined[df_combined['utm_source'] == 'ya-direct']['orders_count'].sum()
      total_revenue_direct = df_combined[df_combined['utm_source'] == 'ya-direct']['total_revenue'].sum()
      total_orders_other = df_combined[df_combined['utm_source'] == 'gdeslon']['orders_count'].sum()
      total_revenue_other = df_combined[df_combined['utm_source'] == 'gdeslon']['total_revenue'].sum()
      
      result += f"\n**Общее сравнение по источникам:**\n"
      result += f"- **Директ (ya-direct):** {total_orders_direct:,} заказов, {total_revenue_direct:,.0f} ₽ выручки\n"
      result += f"- **Другие (gdeslon):** {total_orders_other:,} заказов, {total_revenue_other:,.0f} ₽ выручки\n"
      result += f"- **Соотношение Директ/Другие по заказам:** {total_orders_direct/total_orders_other:.1f}×\n"
      result += f"- **Соотношение Директ/Другие по выручке:** {total_revenue_direct/total_revenue_other:.1f}×\n"
      
      # Анализ различий
      if len(df_comp) > 0:
          direct_dominated = df_comp[df_comp['orders_ya-direct'] > df_comp['orders_gdeslon']].shape[0]
          other_dominated = df_comp[df_comp['orders_gdeslon'] > df_comp['orders_ya-direct']].shape[0]
          equal = df_comp[(df_comp['orders_ya-direct'] == df_comp['orders_gdeslon']) & (df_comp['orders_ya-direct'] > 0)].shape[0]
          
          result += f"\n**Распределение товаров по источникам:**\n"
          result += f"- Лучше продаются в Директе: {direct_dominated} товаров\n"
          result += f"- Лучше продаются из других источников: {other_dominated} товаров\n"
          result += f"- Одинаково хорошо: {equal} товаров\n"
      
      print(f"✅ Проанализировано {len(df_combined)} записей по 2 источникам")
      print(f"📊 Директ: {total_orders_direct} заказов, Другие: {total_orders_other} заказов")
      
      result

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [clickhouse_query]  ~226 tok
    SQL:
      
      WITH purchase_sources AS (
          SELECT 
              arrayJoin(purchaseID) AS pid,
              UTMSource
          FROM visits
          WHERE length(purchaseID) > 0
            AND UTMSource != ''
      ),
      purchases_with_source AS (
          SELECT 
              p.product_name,
              p.product_category,
              p.revenue,
              p.quantity,
              ps.UTMSource,
              CASE WHEN lower(ps.UTMSource) LIKE '%direct%' OR lower(ps.UTMSource) = 'yandex' THEN 'Директ'
                   ELSE 'Другие источники' END AS source_group
          FROM dm_purchases p
          JOIN purchase_sources ps ON toString(p.purchase_id) = ps.pid
      )
      SELECT 
          source_group,
          product_name,
          product_category,
          COUNT() AS orders,
          SUM(revenue) AS total_revenue,
          AVG(revenue) AS avg_check
      FROM purchases_with_source
      GROUP BY source_group, product_name, product_category
      ORDER BY source_group, total_revenue DESC
      LIMIT 200

    SQL:
      
      SELECT 
          j.utm_source,
          p.product_name,
          p.product_category,
          COUNT() AS orders,
          SUM(p.quantity) AS total_qty,
          SUM(p.revenue) AS total_revenue,
          AVG(p.revenue) AS avg_check
      FROM dm_purchases p
      JOIN dm_client_journey j 
          ON p.client_id = j.client_id 
          AND p.date = j.date
          AND j.is_last_before_purchase = 1
      GROUP BY j.utm_source, p.product_name, p.product_category
      ORDER BY total_revenue DESC
      LIMIT 300

    CODE:
      
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      
      df.rename(columns={'j.utm_source': 'utm_source'}, inplace=True)
      
      # Общий топ товаров
      top_overall = df.groupby(['product_name', 'product_category']).agg(
          orders=('orders', 'sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum'),
          avg_check=('avg_check', 'mean')
      ).reset_index().sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False).head(15)
      
      # Разбивка по группам источников
      df['source_group'] = df['utm_source'].apply(
          lambda v: 'Директ (ya-direct)' if str(v).strip() == 'ya-direct' 
          else ('Агрегаторы/другие' if str(v).strip() not in ['', 'nan'] else 'Без UTM')
      )
      
      top_direct = df[df['source_group'] == 'Директ (ya-direct)'].groupby(['product_name', 'product_category']).agg(
          orders=('orders', 'sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum'),
          avg_check=('avg_check', 'mean')
      ).reset_index().sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False).head(10)
      
      top_other = df[df['source_group'] != 'Директ (ya-direct)'].groupby(['product_name', 'product_category']).agg(
          orders=('orders', 'sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum'),
          avg_check=('avg_check', 'mean')
      ).reset_index().sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False).head(10)
      
      # Сколько всего по источникам
      by_source = df.groupby('source_group').agg(
          orders=('orders', 'sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum'),
      ).reset_index()
      by_source['avg_check'] = by_source['total_revenue'] / by_source['orders']
      by_source_sorted = by_source.sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False)
      
      print("Sources distribution:")
      print(by_source_sorted.to_string())
      print("\nTop overall:")
      print(top_overall[['product_name', 'orders', 'total_revenue', 'avg_check']].head(10).to_string())
      
      # Пересечение топ-10 товаров по источникам
      direct_top10 = set(top_direct['product_name'].tolist())
      other_top10 = set(top_other['product_name'].tolist())
      overlap = direct_top10 & other_top10
      print(f"\nПересечение топ-10 Директ vs Другие: {len(overlap)} товаров")
      print(overlap)

      # Полный анализ с визуализацией
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib
      matplotlib.rcParams['font.family'] = 'DejaVu Sans'
      
      # --- Данные для таблиц ---
      
      # Топ-15 товаров по выручке (общий)
      top15 = df.groupby(['product_name', 'product_category']).agg(
          orders=('orders', 'sum'),
          total_qty=('total_qty', 'sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum'),
          avg_check=('avg_check', 'mean')
      ).reset_index().sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False).head(15)
      
      # Топ по Директу
      df_direct = df[df['source_group'] == 'Директ (ya-direct)']
      top_dir = df_direct.groupby(['product_name', 'product_category']).agg(
          orders=('orders', 'sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum'),
          avg_check=('avg_check', 'mean')
      ).reset_index().sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False).head(10)
      
      # Топ по другим
      df_other = df[df['source_group'] != 'Директ (ya-direct)']
      top_oth = df_other.groupby(['product_name', 'product_category']).agg(
          orders=('orders', 'sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum'),
          avg_check=('avg_check', 'mean')
      ).reset_index().sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False).head(10)
      
      # --- График: топ категории по выручке ---
      cat_revenue = df.groupby('product_category')['total_revenue'].sum().sort_values(ascending=True).tail(10)
      
      fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 6))
      bars = ax.barh(cat_revenue.index, cat_revenue.values, color='steelblue')
      ax.set_xlabel('Выручка, руб.', fontsize=11)
      ax.set_title('Топ категорий по выручке', fontsize=13, fontweight='bold')
      for bar, val in zip(bars, cat_revenue.values):
          ax.text(val + cat_revenue.values.max()*0.01, bar.get_y() + bar.get_height()/2,
                  f'{val:,.0f}', va='center', fontsize=9)
      ax.xaxis.set_major_formatter(matplotlib.ticker.FuncFormatter(lambda x, _: f'{x:,.0f}'))
      plt.tight_layout()
      plt.savefig('categories_revenue.png', dpi=120)
      plt.show()
      
      # --- Markdown result ---
      lines = ["## Топ-15 товаров по выручке (all time)\n"]
      lines.append("| # | Товар | Категория | Заказов | Выручка | Ср. чек |")
      lines.append("|---|---|---|---|---|---|")
      for i, row in enumerate(top15.itertuples(), 1):
          name = row.product_name[:50] + ('…' if len(row.product_name) > 50 else '')
          lines.append(f"| {i} | {name} | {row.product_category} | {int(row.orders):,} | {row.total_revenue:,.0f} ₽ | {row.avg_check:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      lines.append("\n---\n")
      lines.append("## Топ товаров — Директ (ya-direct)\n")
      lines.append("| # | Товар | Заказов | Выручка | Ср. чек |")
      lines.append("|---|---|---|---|---|")
      for i, row in enumerate(top_dir.itertuples(), 1):
          name = row.product_name[:55] + ('…' if len(row.product_name) > 55 else '')
          lines.append(f"| {i} | {name} | {int(row.orders):,} | {row.total_revenue:,.0f} ₽ | {row.avg_check:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      lines.append("\n---\n")
      lines.append("## Топ товаров — Другие источники + Без UTM\n")
      lines.append("| # | Товар | Заказов | Выручка | Ср. чек |")
      lines.append("|---|---|---|---|---|")
      for i, row in enumerate(top_oth.itertuples(), 1):
          name = row.product_name[:55] + ('…' if len(row.product_name) > 55 else '')
          lines.append(f"| {i} | {name} | {int(row.orders):,} | {row.total_revenue:,.0f} ₽ | {row.avg_check:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      lines.append("\n---\n")
      lines.append("## Распределение заказов по источникам\n")
      lines.append("| Источник | Заказов | Выручка | Ср. чек |")
      lines.append("|---|---|---|---|")
      for _, row in by_source_sorted.iterrows():
          lines.append(f"| {row['source_group']} | {int(row['orders']):,} | {row['total_revenue']:,.0f} ₽ | {row['avg_check']:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      result = "\n".join(lines)

      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      import matplotlib
      matplotlib.use('Agg')
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      matplotlib.rcParams['font.family'] = 'DejaVu Sans'
      
      df = df.rename(columns={'j.utm_source': 'utm_source'})
      df['utm_source'] = df['utm_source'].fillna('').astype(str).str.strip()
      
      def source_group(s):
          if s == 'ya-direct':
              return 'Директ (ya-direct)'
          elif s == '':
              return 'Без UTM'
          else:
              return 'Другие источники'
      
      df['source_group'] = df['utm_source'].apply(source_group)
      
      # Топ-15 общий
      top15 = df.groupby(['product_name', 'product_category']).agg(
          orders=('orders', 'sum'),
          total_qty=('total_qty', 'sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum')
      ).reset_index()
      top15['avg_check'] = top15['total_revenue'] / top15['orders']
      top15 = top15.sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False).head(15)
      
      # Топ Директ
      top_dir = df[df['source_group'] == 'Директ (ya-direct)'].groupby(['product_name']).agg(
          orders=('orders', 'sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum')
      ).reset_index()
      top_dir['avg_check'] = top_dir['total_revenue'] / top_dir['orders']
      top_dir = top_dir.sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False).head(10)
      
      # Топ другие+без UTM
      top_oth = df[df['source_group'] != 'Директ (ya-direct)'].groupby(['product_name']).agg(
          orders=('orders', 'sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum')
      ).reset_index()
      top_oth['avg_check'] = top_oth['total_revenue'] / top_oth['orders']
      top_oth = top_oth.sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False).head(10)
      
      # Статистика по источникам
      by_source = df.groupby('source_group').agg(orders=('orders','sum'), total_revenue=('total_revenue','sum')).reset_index()
      by_source['avg_check'] = by_source['total_revenue'] / by_source['orders']
      
      # Пересечение
      direct_set = set(top_dir['product_name'])
      other_set = set(top_oth['product_name'])
      overlap = direct_set & other_set
      
      print("Unique sources:", df['utm_source'].unique())
      print("Source groups:\n", df.groupby('source_group')['orders'].sum())
      print("Overlap count:", len(overlap))
      
      # --- График: топ-10 товаров по выручке ---
      top10 = top15.head(10)
      fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 7))
      names_short = [n[:45]+'…' if len(n) > 45 else n for n in top10['product_name']]
      colors = plt.cm.Blues_r(np.linspace(0.3, 0.8, len(top10)))
      bars = ax.barh(names_short[::-1], top10['total_revenue'][::-1].values, color=colors[::-1])
      ax.set_xlabel('Выручка, руб.', fontsize=11)
      ax.set_title('Топ-10 товаров по выручке', fontsize=13, fontweight='bold')
      for bar, val in zip(bars, top10['total_revenue'][::-1].values):
          ax.text(val + top10['total_revenue'].max()*0.01, bar.get_y() + bar.get_height()/2,
                  f'{val:,.0f}', va='center', fontsize=8)
      ax.xaxis.set_major_formatter(matplotlib.ticker.FuncFormatter(lambda x, _: f'{x:,.0f}'))
      plt.tight_layout()
      plt.savefig('top_products.png', dpi=120, bbox_inches='tight')
      plt.show()
      
      # --- Result markdown ---
      lines = []
      lines.append("## Топ-15 товаров по выручке (все источники)\n")
      lines.append("| # | Товар | Заказов | Выручка | Ср. чек |")
      lines.append("|---|---|---|---|---|")
      for i, row in enumerate(top15.itertuples(), 1):
          n = row.product_name[:55] + ('…' if len(row.product_name)>55 else '')
          lines.append(f"| {i} | {n} | {int(row.orders):,} | {row.total_revenue:,.0f} ₽ | {row.avg_check:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      lines.append("\n")
      lines.append("## Распределение заказов по источникам\n")
      lines.append("| Источник | Заказов | Выручка | Ср. чек |")
      lines.append("|---|---|---|---|")
      for _, row in by_source.sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False).iterrows():
          lines.append(f"| {row['source_group']} | {int(row['orders']):,} | {row['total_revenue']:,.0f} ₽ | {row['avg_check']:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      lines.append("\n")
      lines.append("## Топ-10 товаров — Директ (ya-direct)\n")
      lines.append("| # | Товар | Заказов | Выручка | Ср. чек |")
      lines.append("|---|---|---|---|---|")
      for i, row in enumerate(top_dir.itertuples(), 1):
          n = row.product_name[:55] + ('…' if len(row.product_name)>55 else '')
          lines.append(f"| {i} | {n} | {int(row.orders):,} | {row.total_revenue:,.0f} ₽ | {row.avg_check:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      lines.append("\n")
      lines.append("## Топ-10 товаров — Без UTM + Другие источники\n")
      lines.append("| # | Товар | Заказов | Выручка | Ср. чек |")
      lines.append("|---|---|---|---|---|")
      for i, row in enumerate(top_oth.itertuples(), 1):
          n = row.product_name[:55] + ('…' if len(row.product_name)>55 else '')
          lines.append(f"| {i} | {n} | {int(row.orders):,} | {row.total_revenue:,.0f} ₽ | {row.avg_check:,.0f} ₽ |")
      
      lines.append(f"\n**Пересечение топ-10 Директ vs Другие источники:** {len(overlap)} из 10 товаров совпадают")
      if overlap:
          lines.append(f"\nСовпавшие товары: {', '.join([str(p)[:60] for p in overlap])}")
      
      result = "\n".join(lines)

    SQL:
      
      -- Пути клиентов до покупки: топ-5 товаров по выручке
      WITH top_products AS (
          SELECT product_name, SUM(revenue) AS total_revenue
          FROM dm_purchases
          WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 3 MONTH
          GROUP BY product_name
          ORDER BY total_revenue DESC
          LIMIT 5
      ),
      buyers AS (
          SELECT p.client_id, p.product_name, p.revenue, p.date AS purchase_date
          FROM dm_purchases p
          INNER JOIN top_products t ON p.product_name = t.product_name
          WHERE p.date >= today() - INTERVAL 3 MONTH
      )
      SELECT 
          b.product_name,
          b.client_id,
          b.purchase_date,
          COUNT(j.visit_time) AS visits_before_purchase,
          MIN(j.visit_time) AS first_touch,
          MAX(j.visit_time) AS last_touch,
          dateDiff('day', MIN(toDate(j.visit_time)), b.purchase_date) AS days_to_purchase,
          groupArray(j.utm_campaign) AS campaigns,
          groupArray(j.utm_source) AS sources
      FROM buyers b
      LEFT JOIN dm_client_journey j ON b.client_id = j.client_id 
          AND toDate(j.visit_time) <= b.purchase_date
          AND toDate(j.visit_time) >= b.purchase_date - INTERVAL 90 DAY
      GROUP BY b.product_name, b.client_id, b.purchase_date
      LIMIT 2000

      -- Пути клиентов до покупки: топ-5 товаров по выручке

          p.product_name,
          p.client_id,
          p.date AS purchase_date,
          COUNT(j.visit_time) AS visits_before_purchase,
          dateDiff('day', MIN(toDate(j.visit_time)), p.date) AS days_to_purchase,
          groupArray(j.utm_campaign) AS campaigns,
          groupArray(j.utm_source) AS sources
      FROM dm_purchases p
      INNER JOIN (

          FROM dm_purchases
          WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 3 MONTH
          GROUP BY product_name
          ORDER BY tr DESC
          LIMIT 5
      ) top ON p.product_name = top.product_name
      LEFT JOIN dm_client_journey j ON p.client_id = j.client_id 
          AND toDate(j.visit_time) <= p.date
          AND toDate(j.visit_time) >= p.date - INTERVAL 90 DAY
      WHERE p.date >= today() - INTERVAL 3 MONTH
      GROUP BY p.product_name, p.client_id, p.date
      LIMIT 2000

      -- Директ vs органика по категориям: средний чек и повторные покупки

          multiIf(p.utm_source = 'ya-direct', 'ya-direct',
                  p.utm_source = '' OR p.utm_source IS NULL, 'no_utm',
                  'other') AS channel,

      FROM dm_purchases p
      WHERE p.date >= today() - INTERVAL 3 MONTH
      GROUP BY p.product_category, channel
      ORDER BY p.product_category, channel
      LIMIT 500

          SUM(revenue) AS total_revenue,

      # Нормализуем канал
      def norm_channel(s):
          if pd.isna(s) or str(s).strip() == '':
              return 'no_utm'
          s = str(s).strip().lower()

      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      import matplotlib
      matplotlib.use('Agg')
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      import seaborn as sns
      
      # ── Нормализуем канал ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      def norm_channel(s):
          if pd.isna(s) or str(s).strip() == '':
              return 'no_utm'
          s = str(s).strip().lower()
          if s == 'ya-direct':
              return 'ya-direct'
          return 'other'
      
      df['channel'] = df['utm_source'].apply(norm_channel)
      
      # ── Топ-15 по суммарной выручке ───────────────────────────────────────────────
      top15 = (df.groupby('product_name')
               .agg(total_revenue=('total_revenue','sum'), total_orders=('orders','sum'),
                    product_category=('product_category','first'))
               .sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False)
               .head(15)
               .reset_index())
      
      print("Топ-15 получено:", len(top15))
      print(top15[['product_name','total_revenue','total_orders']].head())
      
      # ── Разбивка топ-15 по каналам ────────────────────────────────────────────────
      top15_names = top15['product_name'].tolist()
      df_top15 = df[df['product_name'].isin(top15_names)].copy()
      
      pivot_channel = (df_top15.groupby(['product_name','channel'])['total_revenue']
                       .sum()
                       .unstack(fill_value=0)
                       .reset_index())
      
      # Добавим итоговую выручку для сортировки
      pivot_channel['_total'] = pivot_channel.drop(columns=['product_name']).sum(axis=1)
      pivot_channel = pivot_channel.sort_values('_total', ascending=False)
      
      print("\nPivot каналов:")
      print(pivot_channel.columns.tolist())
      print(pivot_channel.head())

      # Нормализуем utm_source — избегаем pd.isna в apply (тип ArrowDtype)
      df['channel'] = 'no_utm'
      df.loc[df['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() == 'ya-direct', 'channel'] = 'ya-direct'
      df.loc[(df['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() != '') & 
             (df['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() != 'ya-direct') &
             (df['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() != 'None'), 'channel'] = 'other'
      
      print("Каналы:", df['channel'].value_counts().to_dict())
      
      # ── Топ-15 по суммарной выручке ───────────────────────────────────────────────
      top15 = (df.groupby('product_name')
               .agg(total_revenue=('total_revenue','sum'), total_orders=('orders','sum'))
               .sort_values('total_revenue', ascending=False)
               .head(15)
               .reset_index())
      top15_names = top15['product_name'].tolist()
      
      # Добавим категорию
      cat_map = df.groupby('product_name')['product_category'].first()
      top15['category'] = top15['product_name'].map(cat_map)
      
      # ── Разбивка по каналам для топ-15 ────────────────────────────────────────────
      df_top15 = df[df['product_name'].isin(top15_names)].copy()
      df_top15['total_revenue'] = df_top15['total_revenue'].astype(float)
      
      pivot_ch = (df_top15.groupby(['product_name','channel'])['total_revenue']
                  .sum()
                  .unstack(fill_value=0)
                  .reset_index())
      pivot_ch['_total'] = pivot_ch.drop(columns=['product_name']).sum(axis=1)
      pivot_ch = pivot_ch.sort_values('_total', ascending=False)
      
      # Укорачиваем название товара для читаемости
      def short(name, n=45):
          name = str(name).strip()
          return name[:n] + '…' if len(name) > n else name
      
      pivot_ch['short_name'] = pivot_ch['product_name'].apply(short)
      
      print("Pivot готов, колонки:", pivot_ch.columns.tolist())
      print(pivot_ch[['short_name','_total']].head())

      import matplotlib
      matplotlib.use('Agg')
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      
      # ── График 1: Топ-15 по каналам ───────────────────────────────────────────────
      channels_available = [c for c in ['ya-direct', 'no_utm', 'other'] if c in pivot_ch.columns]
      
      fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(13, 7))
      
      colors = {'ya-direct': '#E63946', 'no_utm': '#457B9D', 'other': '#A8DADC'}
      bottom = np.zeros(len(pivot_ch))
      
      for ch in channels_available:
          vals = pivot_ch[ch].values.astype(float)
          bars = ax.barh(pivot_ch['short_name'], vals, left=bottom,
                         label=ch, color=colors.get(ch, '#999'))
          bottom += vals
      
      ax.set_xlabel('Выручка, ₽')
      ax.set_title('Топ-15 товаров по выручке (последние 3 месяца)\nразбивка по каналам', fontsize=13)
      ax.xaxis.set_major_formatter(mticker.FuncFormatter(lambda x, _: f"{x/1e6:.1f}M"))
      ax.invert_yaxis()
      ax.legend(title='Канал', loc='lower right')
      plt.tight_layout()
      plt.savefig('chart_top15.png', dpi=120)
      plt.close()
      
      # ── Таблица топ-15 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      top15_display = pivot_ch[['short_name'] + channels_available + ['_total']].copy()
      # Добавим заказы
      orders_map = df.groupby('product_name')['orders'].sum()
      top15_display['orders'] = top15_display['product_name'].map(orders_map) if 'product_name' in top15_display.columns else ''
      
      # Переименуем
      top15_display_out = pivot_ch.copy()
      top15_display_out['orders'] = top15_display_out['product_name'].map(orders_map)
      top15_display_out['category'] = top15_display_out['product_name'].map(cat_map)
      
      # Форматируем
      rows = []
      for _, r in top15_display_out.iterrows():
          row = {
              'Товар': r['short_name'],
              'Категория': str(r['category'])[:30],
              'Заказов': int(r['orders']),
              'Выручка всего': f"{r['_total']:,.0f}",
              'ya-direct': f"{r.get('ya-direct', 0):,.0f}",
              'no_utm': f"{r.get('no_utm', 0):,.0f}",
          }
          rows.append(row)
      
      df_out = pd.DataFrame(rows)
      md_table = df_out.to_markdown(index=False)
      print("Таблица готова")
      print(df_out.head())

      import matplotlib
      matplotlib.use('Agg')
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      
      # ── Подготовка ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      df['channel'] = 'no_utm'
      df.loc[df['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() == 'ya-direct', 'channel'] = 'ya-direct'
      df.loc[(df['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() != '') & 
             (df['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() != 'ya-direct') &
             (df['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() != 'None'), 'channel'] = 'other'
      
      df['total_revenue'] = df['total_revenue'].astype(float)
      df['orders'] = df['orders'].astype(int)
      
      cat_map = df.groupby('product_name')['product_category'].first()
      orders_map = df.groupby('product_name')['orders'].sum()
      
      top15 = (df.groupby('product_name')['total_revenue'].sum()
               .sort_values(ascending=False).head(15).reset_index())
      top15_names = top15['product_name'].tolist()
      
      df_t = df[df['product_name'].isin(top15_names)].copy()
      
      pivot_ch = (df_t.groupby(['product_name','channel'])['total_revenue']
                  .sum().unstack(fill_value=0).reset_index())
      pivot_ch['_total'] = pivot_ch.drop(columns=['product_name']).sum(axis=1)
      pivot_ch = pivot_ch.sort_values('_total', ascending=False).reset_index(drop=True)
      
      def short(name, n=48):
          name = str(name).strip()
          return name[:n] + '…' if len(name) > n else name
      
      pivot_ch['short_name'] = pivot_ch['product_name'].apply(short)
      pivot_ch['orders']     = pivot_ch['product_name'].map(orders_map)
      pivot_ch['category']   = pivot_ch['product_name'].map(cat_map)
      
      channels_avail = [c for c in ['ya-direct', 'no_utm', 'other'] if c in pivot_ch.columns]

      df_weekly = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_67028b9b7f.parquet')
      df_weekly['week'] = pd.to_datetime(df_weekly['week'])
      df_weekly['total_revenue'] = df_weekly['total_revenue'].astype(float)
      df_weekly['orders'] = df_weekly['orders'].astype(int)
      
      # Категории очень длинные — возьмём первую часть до '/'
      df_weekly['cat_short'] = df_weekly['product_category'].apply(
          lambda x: str(x).split('/')[0].strip()[:40]
      )
      
      # Топ-7 категорий по суммарной выручке
      top_cats = (df_weekly.groupby('cat_short')['total_revenue']
                  .sum().sort_values(ascending=False).head(7).index.tolist())
      
      df_tc = df_weekly[df_weekly['cat_short'].isin(top_cats)].copy()
      weekly_pivot = (df_tc.groupby(['week','cat_short'])['total_revenue']
                      .sum().unstack(fill_value=0))
      
      print("Недели:", weekly_pivot.index.min(), "–", weekly_pivot.index.max())
      print("Категорий:", weekly_pivot.columns.tolist())
      
      # ── Аномалии: z-score по каждой категории ────────────────────────────────────
      anomalies = []
      for cat in weekly_pivot.columns:
          series = weekly_pivot[cat]
          mean_ = series.mean()
          std_  = series.std()
          if std_ == 0:
              continue
          z = (series - mean_) / std_
          for week, z_val in z.items():
              if abs(z_val) > 2:
                  anomalies.append({
                      'Неделя': week.strftime('%d.%m'),
                      'Категория': cat,
                      'Выручка': series[week],
                      'Z-score': round(z_val, 1),
                      'Тип': '▲ всплеск' if z_val > 0 else '▼ провал'
                  })
      
      df_anom = pd.DataFrame(anomalies).sort_values('Z-score', key=abs, ascending=False) if anomalies else pd.DataFrame()
      
      print(f"\nАномалий найдено: {len(df_anom)}")
      print(df_anom.head(10) if len(df_anom) > 0 else "нет аномалий")
      
      # ── График динамики топ-7 категорий ──────────────────────────────────────────
      fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(14, 6))
      palette = sns.color_palette("tab10", len(weekly_pivot.columns))
      import seaborn as sns
      for i, cat in enumerate(weekly_pivot.columns):
          ax.plot(weekly_pivot.index, weekly_pivot[cat], marker='o', markersize=4,
                  label=cat[:35], color=palette[i], linewidth=1.8)
      
      ax.set_title('Еженедельная выручка по топ-7 категориям (3 мес.)', fontsize=13)
      ax.set_xlabel('Неделя')
      ax.set_ylabel('Выручка, ₽')
      ax.yaxis.set_major_formatter(mticker.FuncFormatter(lambda x, _: f"{x/1e6:.1f}M"))
      ax.legend(loc='upper left', fontsize=8, ncol=2)
      plt.xticks(rotation=30)
      plt.tight_layout()
      plt.savefig('chart_weekly.png', dpi=120)
      plt.close()
      
      result = "ok"

      import matplotlib
      matplotlib.use('Agg')
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      import seaborn as sns
      
      # ── Данные Директ vs no_utm по категориям ────────────────────────────────────
      df_cat = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_7f97975770.parquet')
      df_cat['avg_check'] = df_cat['avg_check'].astype(float)
      df_cat['total_revenue'] = df_cat['total_revenue'].astype(float)
      df_cat['orders'] = df_cat['orders'].astype(int)
      
      # Упростим категорию до первого уровня
      df_cat['cat1'] = df_cat['product_category'].apply(lambda x: str(x).split('/')[0].strip())
      
      # Агрегируем по cat1 + channel
      agg = df_cat.groupby(['cat1','channel']).agg(
          orders=('orders','sum'),
          total_revenue=('total_revenue','sum')
      ).reset_index()
      agg['avg_check'] = agg['total_revenue'] / agg['orders']
      
      # Пивот: прямой vs no_utm
      pivot_direct = agg[agg['channel'] == 'ya-direct'][['cat1','avg_check','orders']].rename(
          columns={'avg_check':'direct_avg','orders':'direct_n'})
      pivot_noutm  = agg[agg['channel'] == 'no_utm'][['cat1','avg_check','orders']].rename(
          columns={'avg_check':'noutm_avg','orders':'noutm_n'})
      
      compare = pivot_direct.merge(pivot_noutm, on='cat1', how='outer')
      compare = compare.dropna(subset=['direct_avg','noutm_avg'])  # только с обоими каналами
      compare['ratio'] = compare['direct_avg'] / compare['noutm_avg']
      compare = compare[compare['direct_n'] >= 2]  # мин 2 заказа из Директа
      compare = compare.sort_values('ratio', ascending=False)
      
      print("Сравнение avg_check Директ / no_utm (категории с >= 2 заказа из Директа):")
      print(compare.to_string(index=False))

      import matplotlib
      matplotlib.use('Agg')
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      import seaborn as sns
      
      # ── Аномалии по неделям ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      df_weekly = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_67028b9b7f.parquet')
      df_weekly['week'] = pd.to_datetime(df_weekly['week'])
      df_weekly['total_revenue'] = df_weekly['total_revenue'].astype(float)
      df_weekly['orders'] = df_weekly['orders'].astype(int)
      df_weekly['cat1'] = df_weekly['product_category'].apply(
          lambda x: str(x).split('/')[0].strip()[:45])
      
      top_cats = (df_weekly.groupby('cat1')['total_revenue']
                  .sum().sort_values(ascending=False).head(8).index.tolist())
      df_tc = df_weekly[df_weekly['cat1'].isin(top_cats)].copy()
      weekly_agg = df_tc.groupby(['week','cat1'])['total_revenue'].sum().unstack(fill_value=0)
      
      # Z-score
      anomalies = []
      for cat in weekly_agg.columns:
          series = weekly_agg[cat]
          mean_, std_ = series.mean(), series.std()
          if std_ == 0: continue
          z = (series - mean_) / std_
          for week, z_val in z.items():
              if abs(z_val) > 1.8:
                  anomalies.append({
                      'Неделя': week.strftime('%d.%m.%y'),
                      'Категория': cat[:35],
                      'Выручка, ₽': f"{series[week]:,.0f}",
                      'Z-score': round(z_val, 1),
                      'Тип': '▲ всплеск' if z_val > 0 else '▼ провал'
                  })
      
      df_anom = pd.DataFrame(anomalies).sort_values('Z-score', key=abs, ascending=False) if anomalies else pd.DataFrame()
      print(f"Аномалий: {len(df_anom)}")
      print(df_anom.head(12) if len(df_anom) > 0 else "нет")
      
      # ── График: динамика топ-6 категорий по неделям ──────────────────────────────
      top6 = (df_tc.groupby('cat1')['total_revenue'].sum()
              .sort_values(ascending=False).head(6).index.tolist())
      df_top6 = weekly_agg[top6]
      
      fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(14, 6))
      palette = sns.color_palette("tab10", len(top6))
      for i, cat in enumerate(top6):
          ax.plot(df_top6.index, df_top6[cat], marker='o', markersize=4,
                  label=cat[:32], color=palette[i], linewidth=2)
      
      # Отметим аномалии
      if len(df_anom) > 0:
          for _, row in df_anom.head(6).iterrows():
              # найдём неделю
              pass  # визуально и так видно
      
      ax.set_title('Еженедельная выручка — топ-6 категорий', fontsize=13)
      ax.set_xlabel('Неделя')
      ax.set_ylabel('Выручка, ₽')
      ax.yaxis.set_major_formatter(mticker.FuncFormatter(lambda x, _: f"{x/1e6:.1f} млн"))
      ax.legend(loc='upper left', fontsize=8)
      plt.xticks(rotation=35)
      plt.tight_layout()
      plt.savefig('chart_weekly_cats.png', dpi=120)
      plt.close()
      
      # Markdown аномалий
      if len(df_anom) > 0:
          md_anom = df_anom.head(12).to_markdown(index=False)
      else:
          md_anom = "Аномалий не обнаружено"
      
      result = md_anom

    CODE:
      
      import matplotlib
      matplotlib.use('Agg')
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      
      # ── Директ по кампаниям + категориям ─────────────────────────────────────────
      df_dir = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_13dbfbfde5.parquet')
      df_dir['avg_check'] = df_dir['avg_check'].astype(float)
      df_dir['total_revenue'] = df_dir['total_revenue'].astype(float)
      df_dir['orders'] = df_dir['orders'].astype(int)
      
      # Упростим категорию
      df_dir['cat1'] = df_dir['product_category'].apply(lambda x: str(x).split('/')[0].strip())
      
      # Топ-кампании по выручке (мин 2 заказа)
      top_camp = (df_dir[df_dir['orders'] >= 2]
                  .groupby('utm_campaign')
                  .agg(orders=('orders','sum'), revenue=('total_revenue','sum'),
                       avg_check=('avg_check','mean'))
                  .sort_values('revenue', ascending=False)
                  .head(10)
                  .reset_index())
      
      print("Топ кампаний Директа:")
      print(top_camp.to_string(index=False))
      
      # ── Лучшие кампании для топовых категорий ────────────────────────────────────
      top_cat_direct = (df_dir.groupby('cat1')['total_revenue'].sum()
                        .sort_values(ascending=False).head(5).index.tolist())
      
      df_top_dir = df_dir[df_dir['cat1'].isin(top_cat_direct) & (df_dir['orders'] >= 1)]
      best_by_cat = (df_top_dir.groupby(['cat1','utm_campaign'])
                     .agg(orders=('orders','sum'), revenue=('total_revenue','sum'),
                          avg_check=('avg_check','mean'))
                     .reset_index()
                     .sort_values(['cat1','revenue'], ascending=[True,False]))
      
      # По одной лучшей кампании на категорию
      best1 = best_by_cat.groupby('cat1').first().reset_index()
      print("\nЛучшая кампания на категорию:")
      print(best1.to_string(index=False))
      
      # ── Сравнение avg_check: Директ vs no_utm по категориям ─────────────────────
      df_cat_all = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_7f97975770.parquet')
      df_cat_all['avg_check'] = df_cat_all['avg_check'].astype(float)
      df_cat_all['orders'] = df_cat_all['orders'].astype(int)
      df_cat_all['cat1'] = df_cat_all['product_category'].apply(
          lambda x: str(x).split('/')[0].strip())
      
      agg2 = df_cat_all.groupby(['cat1','channel']).agg(
          n=('orders','sum'), rev=('total_revenue','sum')).reset_index()
      agg2['avg_check'] = agg2['rev'] / agg2['n']
      
      d = agg2[agg2['channel']=='ya-direct'][['cat1','avg_check','n']].rename(
          columns={'avg_check':'direct_avg','n':'direct_n'})
      nu = agg2[agg2['channel']=='no_utm'][['cat1','avg_check','n']].rename(
          columns={'avg_check':'noutm_avg','n':'noutm_n'})
      
      cmp = d.merge(nu, on='cat1', how='inner')
      cmp = cmp[cmp['direct_n'] >= 2]
      cmp['ratio'] = cmp['direct_avg'] / cmp['noutm_avg']
      cmp['diff_pct'] = (cmp['ratio'] - 1) * 100
      cmp = cmp.sort_values('diff_pct', ascending=False)
      
      print("\nСравнение avg_check Директ vs no_utm:")
      print(cmp[['cat1','direct_avg','noutm_avg','direct_n','noutm_n','diff_pct']].to_string(index=False))
      
      result = "ok"

      import matplotlib
      matplotlib.use('Agg')
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      import seaborn as sns
      
      # ── Пути клиентов (топ-5 товаров) ────────────────────────────────────────────
      df_path = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_8dcfc666ac.parquet')
      df_path['visits_before'] = pd.to_numeric(df_path['visits_before'], errors='coerce')
      df_path['days_to_purchase'] = pd.to_numeric(df_path['days_to_purchase'], errors='coerce')
      df_path['unique_campaigns'] = pd.to_numeric(df_path['unique_campaigns'], errors='coerce')
      
      # Краткое имя товара
      def short(name, n=40): return str(name).strip()[:n] + '…' if len(str(name).strip()) > n else str(name).strip()
      df_path['short_name'] = df_path['product_name'].apply(short)
      
      path_agg = (df_path.groupby('short_name').agg(
          n=('visits_before','count'),
          avg_visits=('visits_before','mean'),
          avg_days=('days_to_purchase','mean'),
          avg_campaigns=('unique_campaigns','mean')
      ).reset_index().sort_values('avg_days', ascending=False))
      
      print("Пути клиентов:")
      print(path_agg.to_string(index=False))
      
      # ── График: сравнение avg_check Директ vs no_utm ─────────────────────────────
      df_cat_all = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_7f97975770.parquet')
      df_cat_all['avg_check'] = df_cat_all['avg_check'].astype(float)
      df_cat_all['orders'] = df_cat_all['orders'].astype(int)
      df_cat_all['cat1'] = df_cat_all['product_category'].apply(lambda x: str(x).split('/')[0].strip())
      
      agg2 = df_cat_all.groupby(['cat1','channel']).agg(n=('orders','sum'), rev=('total_revenue','sum')).reset_index()
      agg2['avg_check'] = agg2['rev'] / agg2['n']
      
      d  = agg2[agg2['channel']=='ya-direct'][['cat1','avg_check','n']].rename(columns={'avg_check':'direct','n':'d_n'})
      nu = agg2[agg2['channel']=='no_utm'][['cat1','avg_check','n']].rename(columns={'avg_check':'noutm','n':'nu_n'})
      cmp = d.merge(nu, on='cat1').query('d_n >= 2')
      cmp['diff_pct'] = (cmp['direct'] / cmp['noutm'] - 1) * 100
      cmp = cmp.sort_values('diff_pct', ascending=True)
      
      fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(11, 6))
      colors = ['#E63946' if v > 0 else '#457B9D' for v in cmp['diff_pct']]
      bars = ax.barh(cmp['cat1'], cmp['diff_pct'], color=colors)
      ax.axvline(0, color='black', linewidth=0.8)
      ax.set_xlabel('Разница среднего чека Директ vs no_utm, %')
      ax.set_title('Средний чек из Директа vs без UTM по категориям\n(красный = Директ дороже, синий = Директ дешевле)', fontsize=12)
      for bar, val in zip(bars, cmp['diff_pct']):
          ax.text(val + (5 if val >= 0 else -5), bar.get_y() + bar.get_height()/2,
                  f"{val:+.0f}%", va='center', ha='left' if val >= 0 else 'right', fontsize=9)
      plt.tight_layout()
      plt.savefig('chart_direct_vs_organic.png', dpi=120)
      plt.close()
      
      result = path_agg.to_markdown(index=False)

    CODE:
      
      import matplotlib
      matplotlib.use('Agg')
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      
      # ── Финальный сводный анализ: кампании Директа по топ-категориям ─────────────
      df_dir = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_13dbfbfde5.parquet')
      df_dir['avg_check'] = df_dir['avg_check'].astype(float)
      df_dir['total_revenue'] = df_dir['total_revenue'].astype(float)
      df_dir['orders'] = df_dir['orders'].astype(int)
      df_dir['cat1'] = df_dir['product_category'].apply(lambda x: str(x).split('/')[0].strip())
      def short(name, n=38): return str(name).strip()[:n] + '…' if len(str(name).strip()) > n else str(name).strip()
      df_dir['short_camp'] = df_dir['utm_campaign'].apply(short)
      
      # Топ-5 категорий из Директа
      top5_cats = (df_dir.groupby('cat1')['total_revenue'].sum()
                   .sort_values(ascending=False).head(5).index.tolist())
      
      rows_camp = []
      for cat in top5_cats:
          sub = (df_dir[df_dir['cat1'] == cat]
                 .groupby('short_camp')
                 .agg(orders=('orders','sum'), revenue=('total_revenue','sum'),
                      avg_check=('avg_check','mean'))
                 .sort_values('revenue', ascending=False)
                 .head(3))
          for camp, r in sub.iterrows():
              rows_camp.append({
                  'Категория': cat[:30],
                  'Кампания': camp[:35],
                  'Заказов': int(r['orders']),
                  'Выручка': f"₽{r['revenue']:,.0f}",
                  'Ср.чек': f"₽{r['avg_check']:,.0f}",
              })
      
      df_camp_md = pd.DataFrame(rows_camp)
      
      # ── Аномалии по неделям (финальная таблица) ───────────────────────────────────
      df_weekly = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_67028b9b7f.parquet')
      df_weekly['week'] = pd.to_datetime(df_weekly['week'])
      df_weekly['total_revenue'] = df_weekly['total_revenue'].astype(float)
      df_weekly['orders'] = df_weekly['orders'].astype(int)
      df_weekly['cat1'] = df_weekly['product_category'].apply(lambda x: str(x).split('/')[0].strip()[:45])
      
      top_cats8 = df_weekly.groupby('cat1')['total_revenue'].sum().sort_values(ascending=False).head(8).index
      df_tc = df_weekly[df_weekly['cat1'].isin(top_cats8)]
      wagg = df_tc.groupby(['week','cat1'])['total_revenue'].sum().unstack(fill_value=0)
      
      anomalies = []
      for cat in wagg.columns:
          s = wagg[cat]
          m, sd = s.mean(), s.std()
          if sd == 0: continue
          z = (s - m) / sd
          for wk, zv in z.items():
              if abs(zv) > 1.8:
                  anomalies.append({
                      'Неделя': wk.strftime('%d.%m.%y'),
                      'Категория': cat[:35],
                      'Выручка': f"₽{s[wk]:,.0f}",
                      'Z': round(zv,1),
                      'Тип': '▲ всплеск' if zv > 0 else '▼ провал'
                  })
      
      df_anom = pd.DataFrame(anomalies).sort_values('Z', key=abs, ascending=False) if anomalies else pd.DataFrame()
      
      # ── Топ-15 итоговая таблица ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
      df_sales = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_8c2c070e17.parquet')
      df_sales['channel'] = 'no_utm'
      df_sales.loc[df_sales['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() == 'ya-direct', 'channel'] = 'ya-direct'
      df_sales.loc[(df_sales['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() != '') & 
                   (df_sales['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() != 'ya-direct') &
                   (df_sales['utm_source'].astype(str).str.strip() != 'None'), 'channel'] = 'other'
      df_sales['total_revenue'] = df_sales['total_revenue'].astype(float)
      df_sales['orders'] = df_sales['orders'].astype(int)
      
      cat_map = df_sales.groupby('product_name')['product_category'].first()
      orders_map = df_sales.groupby('product_name')['orders'].sum()
      top15 = df_sales.groupby('product_name')['total_revenue'].sum().sort_values(ascending=False).head(15)
      
      pivot_ch = (df_sales[df_sales['product_name'].isin(top15.index)]
                  .groupby(['product_name','channel'])['total_revenue'].sum()
                  .unstack(fill_value=0).reset_index())
      pivot_ch['_total'] = pivot_ch.drop(columns=['product_name']).sum(axis=1)
      pivot_ch = pivot_ch.sort_values('_total', ascending=False)
      pivot_ch['short'] = pivot_ch['product_name'].apply(lambda n: str(n).strip()[:50] + '…' if len(str(n).strip())>50 else str(n).strip())
      pivot_ch['cat'] = pivot_ch['product_name'].map(cat_map).apply(lambda x: str(x).split('/')[0].strip()[:25])
      pivot_ch['orders'] = pivot_ch['product_name'].map(orders_map)
      
      # Форматируем для markdown
      t15_rows = []
      for i, (_, r) in enumerate(pivot_ch.iterrows(), 1):
          t15_rows.append({
              '#': i,
              'Товар': r['short'],
              'Категория': r['cat'],
              'Зак.': int(r['orders']),
              'Выручка': f"₽{r['_total']:,.0f}",
              'Директ': f"₽{r.get('ya-direct',0):,.0f}",
              'no_utm': f"₽{r.get('no_utm',0):,.0f}",
          })
      md_top15 = pd.DataFrame(t15_rows).to_markdown(index=False)
      
      # Пересечение топ-10
      direct_top10 = set(df_sales[df_sales['channel']=='ya-direct'].groupby('product_name')['total_revenue']
                         .sum().sort_values(ascending=False).head(10).index)
      organic_top10 = set(df_sales[df_sales['channel']=='no_utm'].groupby('product_name')['total_revenue']
                          .sum().sort_values(ascending=False).head(10).index)
      overlap = direct_top10 & organic_top10
      
      # ── Сравнение avg_check ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      df_cat_all = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_7f97975770.parquet')
      df_cat_all['avg_check'] = df_cat_all['avg_check'].astype(float)
      df_cat_all['orders'] = df_cat_all['orders'].astype(int)
      df_cat_all['total_revenue'] = df_cat_all['total_revenue'].astype(float)
      df_cat_all['cat1'] = df_cat_all['product_category'].apply(lambda x: str(x).split('/')[0].strip())
      
      agg2 = df_cat_all.groupby(['cat1','channel']).agg(n=('orders','sum'), rev=('total_revenue','sum')).reset_index()
      agg2['avg_check'] = agg2['rev'] / agg2['n']
      d  = agg2[agg2['channel']=='ya-direct'][['cat1','avg_check','n']].rename(columns={'avg_check':'direct','n':'d_n'})
      nu = agg2[agg2['channel']=='no_utm'][['cat1','avg_check','n']].rename(columns={'avg_check':'noutm','n':'nu_n'})
      cmp = d.merge(nu, on='cat1').query('d_n >= 2')
      cmp['diff_pct'] = (cmp['direct'] / cmp['noutm'] - 1) * 100
      cmp = cmp.sort_values('diff_pct', ascending=False)
      cmp_rows = []
      for _, r in cmp.iterrows():
          cmp_rows.append({
              'Категория': r['cat1'][:32],
              'Директ ср.чек': f"₽{r['direct']:,.0f}",
              'no_utm ср.чек': f"₽{r['noutm']:,.0f}",
              'Директ зак.': int(r['d_n']),
              'no_utm зак.': int(r['nu_n']),
              'Разница': f"{r['diff_pct']:+.0f}%",
          })
      md_cmp = pd.DataFrame(cmp_rows).to_markdown(index=False)
      
      # ── Финальный result ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      md_anom = df_anom.head(10).to_markdown(index=False) if len(df_anom) > 0 else "_Аномалий не обнаружено_"
      md_camp = df_camp_md.to_markdown(index=False) if len(df_camp_md) > 0 else "_Нет данных_"
      
      result = f"""
      ## 1. Топ-15 товаров за 3 месяца — разбивка по каналам
      
      {md_top15}
      
      **Пересечение топ-10 Директ ∩ no_utm:** {len(overlap)} {'товаров' if len(overlap) != 1 else 'товар'}{': ' + ', '.join([str(n)[:40] for n in overlap]) if overlap else ''}
      
      ---
      
      ## 3. Средний чек: ya-direct vs no_utm по категориям
      
      {md_cmp}
      
      ---
      
      ## 4. Аномалии в продажах по неделям
      
      {md_anom}
      
      ---
      
      ## 5. Лучшие кампании ya-direct по топовым категориям
      
      {md_camp}
      """

    ## Что я умею  Я аналитик рекламных данных, работаю напрямую с вашей
    ClickHouse-базой. Вот мои основные направления:  ---  ### Трафик и источники
    - Визиты, сессии, новые пользователи по
    источникам/кампаниям/устройствам/городам - Динамика трафика во времени,
    сравнение периодов - Поиск аномалий: провалы, всплески, подозрительные
    источники  ### Кампании и воронка - Эффективность кампаний: CR, bounce rate,
    глубина просмотра, длительность - Сравнение utm_source / utm_campaign по
    любым метрикам - Откуда приходят покупатели vs просто посетители  ###
    Покупки и выручка - Топ продуктов, категорий, источников по revenue -
    Средний чек, количество покупок, LTV-срезы - Связка «кампания → покупка»
    ### Поведение клиентов - Путь клиента от первого визита до покупки - Сколько
    визитов до конверсии, какие каналы участвуют - Сегменты: новые vs
    возвращающиеся, одноразовые vs повторные покупатели  ### Атрибуция и
    conversion paths - First touch / last touch по источникам и кампаниям -
    Длина пути, окно конверсии - Какие комбинации каналов ведут к покупке  ###
    Профили клиентов - Активность, давность визита, история покупок -
    Сегментация по устройству, городу, источнику привлечения  ---  **Как
    работать:** просто задавай вопросы в свободной форме — «почему упал трафик с
    Яндекса», «топ кампаний за месяц», «сравни мобиль и десктоп по конверсии». Я
    сам составляю запросы, нахожу аномалии и предлагаю следующий шаг.

  🤖 AI_ANSWER  ~195 tok
    У меня уже есть схема базы данных — все таблицы описаны в промпте:
    **Основные таблицы:** 1. **dm_campaign_funnel** — воронка по кампаниям (UTM-
    метки, визиты, конверсии, выручка) 2. **dm_client_journey** — путь клиента
    (история визитов, события покупок) 3. **dm_client_profile** — профили
    клиентов (метрики активности, покупки, атрибуты) 4. **dm_conversion_paths**
    — пути конверсий (вся история каналов до покупки) 5. **dm_purchases** —
    детали покупок 6. **dm_traffic_performance** — производительность трафика по
    дням и атрибутам 7. **visits** — сырые данные визитов  **Справочная
    информация:** - deviceCategory: 1=десктоп, 2=мобильные, 3=планшеты, 4=TV -
    Визиты в dm_traffic_performance включают анонимные (clientID=0), другие
    витрины — только clientID>0  Что будем анализировать?

      -- Визиты за последний месяц (последние 30 дней)
      SELECT 
          date,
          COUNT() as visits_count,
          COUNTIf(clientID > 0) as visits_with_client_id,
          COUNTIf(clientID = 0) as anonymous_visits,
          AVG(visitDuration) as avg_duration_sec,
          SUM(bounce) as bounces,
          SUM(pageViews) as total_pageviews
      FROM visits 
      WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 30 DAY
      GROUP BY date
      ORDER BY date

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [clickhouse_query]  ~363 tok
    SQL:
      
      -- Шаг 1: когорта + первая и вторая покупка
      WITH segment AS (
          SELECT client_id
          FROM (
              SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_purchase_date
              FROM dm_purchases
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING first_purchase_date BETWEEN '2025-06-01' AND '2025-08-31'
          ) AS fp
          INNER JOIN dm_client_profile AS cp USING (client_id)
          WHERE cp.first_utm_source IN ('', 'direct')
      ),
      purchase_dates AS (
          SELECT
              p.client_id,
              min(p.date) AS first_purchase_date,
              groupArray(p.date) AS all_dates
          FROM dm_purchases p
          INNER JOIN segment s USING (client_id)
          GROUP BY p.client_id
      ),
      cohort AS (
          SELECT
              client_id,
              first_purchase_date,
              arraySort(all_dates) AS sorted_dates,
              -- вторая покупка (если есть)
              if(length(arraySort(all_dates)) >= 2, arraySort(all_dates)[2], toDate('1970-01-01')) AS second_purchase_date
          FROM purchase_dates
      ),
      cohort_labeled AS (
          SELECT
              client_id,
              first_purchase_date,
              second_purchase_date,
              CASE
                  WHEN second_purchase_date != toDate('1970-01-01')
                   AND dateDiff('day', first_purchase_date, second_purchase_date) <= 90
                  THEN 1 ELSE 0
              END AS returned_90d
          FROM cohort
      )
      SELECT
          client_id,
          first_purchase_date,
          second_purchase_date,
          returned_90d
      FROM cohort_labeled
      LIMIT 500000

      WITH segment AS (
          SELECT client_id
          FROM (
              SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_purchase_date
              FROM dm_purchases
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING first_purchase_date BETWEEN '2025-06-01' AND '2025-08-31'
          ) AS fp
          INNER JOIN dm_client_profile AS cp USING (client_id)
          WHERE cp.first_utm_source IN ('', 'direct')
      ),
      purchase_dates AS (
          SELECT
              p.client_id,
              arraySort(groupArray(p.date)) AS sorted_dates,
              min(p.date) AS first_purchase_date
          FROM dm_purchases p
          INNER JOIN segment s USING (client_id)
          GROUP BY p.client_id
      ),
      cohort_labeled AS (
          SELECT
              client_id,
              first_purchase_date,
              sorted_dates[2] AS second_purchase_date,
              CASE
                  WHEN length(sorted_dates) >= 2
                   AND dateDiff('day', first_purchase_date, sorted_dates[2]) <= 90
                  THEN 1 ELSE 0
              END AS returned_90d
          FROM purchase_dates
      )
      SELECT
          cl.client_id,
          cl.first_purchase_date,
          cl.second_purchase_date,
          cl.returned_90d
      FROM cohort_labeled cl
      LIMIT 500000

    SQL:
      
      SELECT
          p.client_id,
          min(p.date) AS first_purchase_date,
          arraySort(groupArray(p.date))[2] AS second_purchase_date,
          if(
              length(arraySort(groupArray(p.date))) >= 2
              AND dateDiff('day', min(p.date), arraySort(groupArray(p.date))[2]) <= 90,
              1, 0
          ) AS returned_90d
      FROM dm_purchases p
      INNER JOIN (
          SELECT fp.client_id
          FROM (
              SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_purchase_date
              FROM dm_purchases
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING first_purchase_date BETWEEN '2025-06-01' AND '2025-08-31'
          ) AS fp

          WHERE cp.first_utm_source IN ('', 'direct')
      ) AS seg ON p.client_id = seg.client_id
      GROUP BY p.client_id
      LIMIT 500000

      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      
      # Загрузим когорту (уже в df — это journey)
      journey = df.copy()
      journey['date'] = pd.to_datetime(journey['date'])
