      cohort = pd.read_parquet('/root/clickhouse_analytics_agent/temp_data/query_baddc5e3e6.parquet')
      cohort['first_purchase_date'] = pd.to_datetime(cohort['first_purchase_date'])
      cohort['second_purchase_date'] = pd.to_datetime(cohort['second_purchase_date'])
      
      print(f"Когорта: {len(cohort)} клиентов")
      print(f"Вернулись (90д): {cohort['returned_90d'].sum()}")
      print(f"Не вернулись: {(cohort['returned_90d']==0).sum()}")
      print(f"Визитов в journey: {len(journey)}")
      
      # Присоединим метку returned_90d к journey
      journey = journey.merge(cohort[['client_id','first_purchase_date','second_purchase_date','returned_90d']], on='client_id', how='left')
      
      # Оставим только визиты ПОСЛЕ первой покупки
      # Для вернувшихся — до даты второй покупки
      journey_post = journey[journey['date'] > journey['first_purchase_date']].copy()
      
      # Для вернувшихся — ограничим периодом до второй покупки (включительно)
      returned_mask = journey_post['returned_90d'] == 1
      not_returned_mask = journey_post['returned_90d'] == 0
      
      # У вернувшихся — окно до second_purchase_date
      journey_returned = journey_post[returned_mask].copy()
      journey_returned = journey_returned[journey_returned['date'] <= journey_returned['second_purchase_date']]
      
      # У невернувшихся — окно 90 дней после первой покупки
      journey_not_ret = journey_post[not_returned_mask].copy()
      journey_not_ret = journey_not_ret[journey_not_ret['date'] <= journey_not_ret['first_purchase_date'] + pd.Timedelta(days=90)]
      
      print(f"\nВизиты после первой покупки:")
      print(f"  Вернувшиеся (клиентов {cohort['returned_90d'].sum()}): {len(journey_returned)} визитов")
      print(f"  Невернувшиеся: {len(journey_not_ret)} визитов")
      
      # --- 1. Среднее количество визитов ---
      visits_returned = journey_returned.groupby('client_id').size().reset_index(name='visits')
      visits_not_ret = journey_not_ret.groupby('client_id').size().reset_index(name='visits')
      
      # Добавим нули для тех, у кого нет визитов
      all_returned_ids = cohort[cohort['returned_90d']==1]['client_id']
      all_not_ret_ids = cohort[cohort['returned_90d']==0]['client_id']
      
      visits_returned_full = pd.DataFrame({'client_id': all_returned_ids}).merge(visits_returned, on='client_id', how='left').fillna(0)
      visits_not_ret_full = pd.DataFrame({'client_id': all_not_ret_ids}).merge(visits_not_ret, on='client_id', how='left').fillna(0)
      
      avg_ret = visits_returned_full['visits'].mean()
      avg_not = visits_not_ret_full['visits'].mean()
      med_ret = visits_returned_full['visits'].median()
      med_not = visits_not_ret_full['visits'].median()
      
      print(f"\nСреднее визитов:")
      print(f"  Вернулись: {avg_ret:.1f} (медиана {med_ret:.1f})")
      print(f"  Не вернулись: {avg_not:.1f} (медиана {med_not:.1f})")
      
      # --- 2. Bounce rate ---
      br_ret = journey_returned['bounce'].mean() if len(journey_returned) > 0 else np.nan
      br_not = journey_not_ret['bounce'].mean() if len(journey_not_ret) > 0 else np.nan
      
      # --- 3. Среднее page_views и visit_duration ---
      pv_ret = journey_returned['page_views'].mean()
      pv_not = journey_not_ret['page_views'].mean()
      
      dur_ret = journey_returned['visit_duration'].mean()
      dur_not = journey_not_ret['visit_duration'].mean()
      
      # --- 4. UTM source для вернувшихся ---
      utm_ret = journey_returned['utm_source'].replace('', 'direct/organic').value_counts()
      print(f"\nUTM source (вернувшиеся):\n{utm_ret}")
      
      utm_not = journey_not_ret['utm_source'].replace('', 'direct/organic').value_counts(normalize=True).head(5)
      print(f"\nUTM source (не вернулись, %):\n{utm_not}")
      
      # --- 5. График: визиты ---
      fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(12, 5))
      
      # Гистограмма визитов
      ax1 = axes[0]
      bins = range(0, int(max(visits_returned_full['visits'].max(), visits_not_ret_full['visits'].max())) + 2)
      ax1.hist(visits_returned_full['visits'], bins=bins, alpha=0.7, label=f'Вернулись (n={len(all_returned_ids)})', color='#2ecc71', edgecolor='white')
      ax1.hist(visits_not_ret_full['visits'], bins=bins, alpha=0.5, label=f'Не вернулись (n={len(all_not_ret_ids)})', color='#e74c3c', edgecolor='white')
      ax1.set_xlabel('Визитов после первой покупки')
      ax1.set_ylabel('Клиентов')
      ax1.set_title('Распределение визитов (до 2-й покупки / 90 дней)')
      ax1.legend()
      ax1.set_xlim(0, 20)
      
      # Bar chart сравнения метрик
      ax2 = axes[1]
      metrics = ['Avg визитов', 'Bounce rate', 'Avg страниц', 'Avg длит., мин']
      vals_ret = [avg_ret, br_ret * 100, pv_ret, dur_ret / 60]
      vals_not = [avg_not, br_not * 100, pv_not, dur_not / 60]
      
      x = np.arange(len(metrics))
      w = 0.35
      bars1 = ax2.bar(x - w/2, vals_ret, w, label='Вернулись', color='#2ecc71')
      bars2 = ax2.bar(x + w/2, vals_not, w, label='Не вернулись', color='#e74c3c')
      ax2.set_xticks(x)
      ax2.set_xticklabels(metrics, fontsize=9)
      ax2.set_title('Поведенческие метрики визитов')
      ax2.legend()
      
      plt.tight_layout()
      plt.savefig('cohort_visits_comparison.png', dpi=130)
      plt.show()
      
      # --- Итоговая таблица ---
      result = f"""## Вернулись vs не вернулись — визиты после первой покупки
      
      **Окно анализа:** вернувшиеся — до даты 2-й покупки; не вернувшиеся — 90 дней после 1-й покупки.
      
      ### Активность визитов
      
      | Метрика | Вернулись (n={int(len(all_returned_ids))}) | Не вернулись (n={int(len(all_not_ret_ids))}) |
      |---|---|---|
      | Среднее визитов | **{avg_ret:.1f}** | {avg_not:.1f} |
      | Медиана визитов | {med_ret:.1f} | {med_not:.1f} |
      | Bounce rate | {br_ret:.1%} | {br_not:.1%} |
      | Avg страниц/визит | {pv_ret:.1f} | {pv_not:.1f} |
      | Avg длительность | {dur_ret/60:.1f} мин | {dur_not/60:.1f} мин |
      
      ### UTM-источники визитов (вернувшиеся, абс.)
      
      | Источник | Визитов |
      |---|---|
      """
      for src, cnt in utm_ret.items():
          result += f"| {src} | {cnt:,} |\n"
      
      result += f"""
      ### Интерпретация
      - Вернувшиеся делали в среднем **{avg_ret:.1f} визита** против {avg_not:.1f} у невернувшихся — в {avg_ret/avg_not:.1f}x больше активности
      - Bounce rate вернувшихся **ниже на {(br_not - br_ret):.1%}** — более целенаправленное поведение
      - Страниц за визит у вернувшихся больше ({pv_ret:.1f} vs {pv_not:.1f}) — глубже изучают контент
      """
      print(result)

    SQL:
      
      WITH segment AS (
          SELECT DISTINCT fp.client_id
          FROM (
              SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_purchase_date
              FROM dm_purchases
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING first_purchase_date BETWEEN '2025-06-01' AND '2025-08-31'
          ) AS fp
          INNER JOIN dm_client_profile AS cp ON fp.client_id = cp.client_id
          WHERE cp.first_utm_source IN ('', 'direct')
      ),
      purchases AS (
          SELECT
              p.client_id,
              p.date,
              row_number() OVER (PARTITION BY p.client_id ORDER BY p.date) AS purchase_num
          FROM dm_purchases p
          INNER JOIN segment s ON p.client_id = s.client_id
      ),
      first_second AS (
          SELECT
              client_id,
              min(if(purchase_num = 1, date, NULL)) AS first_date,
              min(if(purchase_num = 2, date, NULL)) AS second_date
          FROM purchases
          GROUP BY client_id
          HAVING second_date IS NOT NULL
             AND second_date <= first_date + INTERVAL 90 DAY
      ),
      days_calc AS (
          SELECT
              client_id,
              toInt32(dateDiff('day', first_date, second_date)) AS days_to_repeat
          FROM first_second
      )
      SELECT
          days_to_repeat,
          count() AS clients
      FROM days_calc
      WHERE days_to_repeat BETWEEN 1 AND 90
      GROUP BY days_to_repeat
      ORDER BY days_to_repeat
      LIMIT 90

    SQL:
      
      WITH segment AS (
          SELECT DISTINCT fp.client_id
          FROM (
              SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_purchase_date
              FROM dm_purchases
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING first_purchase_date BETWEEN '2025-06-01' AND '2025-08-31'
          ) AS fp
          INNER JOIN dm_client_profile AS cp ON fp.client_id = cp.client_id
          WHERE cp.first_utm_source IN ('', 'direct')
      ),
      purchases AS (
          SELECT
              p.client_id,
              p.date,
              row_number() OVER (PARTITION BY p.client_id ORDER BY p.date) AS purchase_num
          FROM dm_purchases p
          INNER JOIN segment s ON p.client_id = s.client_id
      ),
      first_second AS (
          SELECT
              client_id,
              minIf(date, purchase_num = 1) AS first_date,
              minIf(date, purchase_num = 2) AS second_date
          FROM purchases
          GROUP BY client_id
          HAVING second_date != toDate('1970-01-01')
             AND second_date <= first_date + INTERVAL 90 DAY
             AND second_date > first_date
      )
      SELECT
          dateDiff('day', first_date, second_date) AS days_to_repeat,
          count() AS clients
      FROM first_second
      WHERE days_to_repeat BETWEEN 1 AND 90
      GROUP BY days_to_repeat
      ORDER BY days_to_repeat
      LIMIT 90

    SQL:
      
      WITH segment AS (
          SELECT DISTINCT fp.client_id
          FROM (
              SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_purchase_date
              FROM dm_purchases
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING first_purchase_date BETWEEN '2025-06-01' AND '2025-08-31'
          ) AS fp
          INNER JOIN dm_client_profile cp ON fp.client_id = cp.client_id
          WHERE cp.first_utm_source IN ('', 'direct')
      ),
      purchases_ranked AS (
          SELECT
              p.client_id,
              p.date,
              row_number() OVER (PARTITION BY p.client_id ORDER BY p.date ASC) AS purchase_num
          FROM dm_purchases p
          WHERE p.client_id IN (SELECT client_id FROM segment)
      ),
      first_dates AS (
          SELECT client_id, date AS first_date
          FROM purchases_ranked
          WHERE purchase_num = 1
      ),
      second_dates AS (
          SELECT client_id, date AS second_date
          FROM purchases_ranked
          WHERE purchase_num = 2
      ),
      joined AS (
          SELECT
              f.client_id,
              f.first_date,
              s.second_date,
              dateDiff('day', f.first_date, s.second_date) AS days_to_repeat
          FROM first_dates f
          INNER JOIN second_dates s ON f.client_id = s.client_id
          WHERE s.second_date > f.first_date
            AND dateDiff('day', f.first_date, s.second_date) <= 90
      )
      SELECT days_to_repeat, count() AS clients
      FROM joined
      WHERE days_to_repeat >= 1
      GROUP BY days_to_repeat
      ORDER BY days_to_repeat
      LIMIT 90

      WITH segment AS (
          SELECT DISTINCT fp.client_id
          FROM (
              SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_purchase_date
              FROM dm_purchases
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING first_purchase_date BETWEEN '2025-06-01' AND '2025-08-31'
          ) AS fp
          INNER JOIN dm_client_profile cp ON fp.client_id = cp.client_id
          WHERE cp.first_utm_source IN ('', 'direct')
      ),
      first_purchases AS (
          SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_date
          FROM dm_purchases
          WHERE client_id IN (SELECT client_id FROM segment)
          GROUP BY client_id
      ),
      second_purchases AS (
          SELECT p.client_id, min(p.date) AS second_date
          FROM dm_purchases p
          INNER JOIN first_purchases fp ON p.client_id = fp.client_id
          WHERE p.date > fp.first_date
          GROUP BY p.client_id
      )
      SELECT
          dateDiff('day', fp.first_date, sp.second_date) AS days_to_repeat,
          count() AS clients
      FROM first_purchases fp
      INNER JOIN second_purchases sp ON fp.client_id = sp.client_id
      WHERE dateDiff('day', fp.first_date, sp.second_date) BETWEEN 1 AND 90
      GROUP BY days_to_repeat
      ORDER BY days_to_repeat
      LIMIT 90

      SELECT
          dateDiff('day', fp.first_date, sp.second_date) AS days_to_repeat,
          count() AS clients
      FROM (
          SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_date
          FROM dm_purchases
          WHERE client_id IN (
              SELECT DISTINCT fp2.client_id
              FROM (
                  SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_purchase_date
                  FROM dm_purchases
                  GROUP BY client_id
                  HAVING first_purchase_date BETWEEN '2025-06-01' AND '2025-08-31'
              ) AS fp2
              INNER JOIN dm_client_profile cp ON fp2.client_id = cp.client_id
              WHERE cp.first_utm_source IN ('', 'direct')
          )
          GROUP BY client_id
      ) AS fp
      INNER JOIN (
          SELECT p.client_id, min(p.date) AS second_date
          FROM dm_purchases p
          INNER JOIN (
              SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_date
              FROM dm_purchases
              WHERE client_id IN (
                  SELECT DISTINCT fp3.client_id
                  FROM (
                      SELECT client_id, min(date) AS first_purchase_date
                      FROM dm_purchases
                      GROUP BY client_id
                      HAVING first_purchase_date BETWEEN '2025-06-01' AND '2025-08-31'
                  ) AS fp3
                  INNER JOIN dm_client_profile cp ON fp3.client_id = cp.client_id
                  WHERE cp.first_utm_source IN ('', 'direct')
              )
              GROUP BY client_id
          ) AS fp4 ON p.client_id = fp4.client_id
          WHERE p.date > fp4.first_date
          GROUP BY p.client_id
      ) AS sp ON fp.client_id = sp.client_id
      WHERE dateDiff('day', fp.first_date, sp.second_date) BETWEEN 1 AND 90
      GROUP BY days_to_repeat
      ORDER BY days_to_repeat
      LIMIT 90

    CODE:
      
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      import numpy as np
      
      # Заполним пропущенные дни нулями
      all_days = pd.DataFrame({'days_to_repeat': range(1, 91)})
      df_full = all_days.merge(df, on='days_to_repeat', how='left').fillna(0)
      df_full['clients'] = df_full['clients'].astype(int)
      
      # Накопленный %
      total = df_full['clients'].sum()
      df_full['cumsum'] = df_full['clients'].cumsum()
      df_full['cum_pct'] = df_full['cumsum'] / total * 100
      
      # Ключевые пороги
      d7  = df_full[df_full['days_to_repeat'] <= 7]['clients'].sum()
      d14 = df_full[df_full['days_to_repeat'] <= 14]['clients'].sum()
      d30 = df_full[df_full['days_to_repeat'] <= 30]['clients'].sum()
      d60 = df_full[df_full['days_to_repeat'] <= 60]['clients'].sum()
      d90 = total
      
      print(f"Total returnees: {total}")
      print(f"≤7 дней:  {d7} ({d7/total:.1%})")
      print(f"≤14 дней: {d14} ({d14/total:.1%})")
      print(f"≤30 дней: {d30} ({d30/total:.1%})")
      print(f"≤60 дней: {d60} ({d60/total:.1%})")
      
      # Топ-5 дней
      top5 = df_full[df_full['clients'] > 0].nlargest(5, 'clients')[['days_to_repeat', 'clients']]
      print("\nТоп-5 дней:")
      print(top5.to_string())
      
      # --- График ---
      fig, ax1 = plt.subplots(figsize=(14, 6))
      
      # Бары по неделям — группируем
      colors = []
      for d in df_full['days_to_repeat']:
          if d <= 7:   colors.append('#2196F3')
          elif d <= 14: colors.append('#4CAF50')
          elif d <= 30: colors.append('#FF9800')
          elif d <= 60: colors.append('#9C27B0')
          else:         colors.append('#F44336')
      
      ax1.bar(df_full['days_to_repeat'], df_full['clients'], color=colors, alpha=0.85, width=0.8)
      ax1.set_xlabel('День после первой покупки', fontsize=12)
      ax1.set_ylabel('Количество клиентов', fontsize=12)
      ax1.set_title('Когорта organic_first: когда вернулись за второй покупкой (90 дней)', fontsize=14)
      ax1.yaxis.set_major_formatter(mticker.FuncFormatter(lambda x, _: f"{x:,.0f}"))
      
      # Накопленная кривая
      ax2 = ax1.twinx()
      ax2.plot(df_full['days_to_repeat'], df_full['cum_pct'], color='black', linewidth=2, label='Накопленный %')
      ax2.set_ylabel('Накопленный %', fontsize=12)
      ax2.set_ylim(0, 110)

    SQL:
      
      -- Средний интервал между покупками для сегмента hv_desktop_moscow
      WITH segment AS (
          SELECT DISTINCT buyers.client_id
          FROM (
              SELECT
                  client_id,
                  count()      AS purchase_count,
                  sum(revenue) AS total_revenue
              FROM dm_purchases
              WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 180 DAY
                AND city = 'Moscow'
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING purchase_count >= 2
                 AND total_revenue / purchase_count > 15000
          ) buyers
          INNER JOIN dm_client_profile cp ON cp.client_id = buyers.client_id
          WHERE cp.last_device = '1'
      ),
      purchase_dates AS (
          SELECT
              p.client_id,
              p.date,
              lagInFrame(p.date) OVER (PARTITION BY p.client_id ORDER BY p.date) AS prev_date
          FROM dm_purchases p
          INNER JOIN segment s ON s.client_id = p.client_id
          WHERE p.date >= today() - INTERVAL 180 DAY
      )
      SELECT
          count()                                          AS intervals_count,
          round(avg(dateDiff('day', prev_date, date)), 1)  AS avg_interval_days,
          round(median(dateDiff('day', prev_date, date)), 1) AS median_interval_days,
          min(dateDiff('day', prev_date, date))            AS min_interval_days,
          max(dateDiff('day', prev_date, date))            AS max_interval_days
      FROM purchase_dates
      WHERE prev_date IS NOT NULL
      LIMIT 1

                  sum(revenue) AS total_revenue
              FROM dm_purchases
              WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 180 DAY
                AND city = 'Moscow'
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING purchase_count >= 2
                 AND total_revenue / purchase_count > 15000
          ) buyers

      SELECT
          cj.utm_source,
          count()                            AS visits,
          count(DISTINCT cj.client_id)       AS clients,
          round(avg(cj.visit_duration), 0)   AS avg_duration_sec,
          round(avg(cj.page_views), 1)       AS avg_pageviews
      FROM dm_client_journey cj
      INNER JOIN segment s ON s.client_id = cj.client_id
      WHERE cj.is_last_before_purchase = 1
      GROUP BY cj.utm_source
      ORDER BY visits DESC
      LIMIT 50

      WITH segment AS (
          SELECT DISTINCT buyers.client_id
          FROM (
              SELECT
                  client_id,
                  count()      AS purchase_count,
                  sum(revenue) AS total_revenue
              FROM dm_purchases
              WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 180 DAY
                AND city = 'Moscow'
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING purchase_count >= 2
                 AND total_revenue / purchase_count > 15000
          ) buyers
          INNER JOIN dm_client_profile cp ON cp.client_id = buyers.client_id
          WHERE cp.last_device = '1'
      ),
      client_purchase_dates AS (
          SELECT
              p.client_id,
              groupArray(p.date) AS dates
          FROM dm_purchases p
          INNER JOIN segment s ON s.client_id = p.client_id
          WHERE p.date >= today() - INTERVAL 180 DAY
          GROUP BY p.client_id
          HAVING length(dates) >= 2
      )
      SELECT
          sum(length(dates) - 1)           AS intervals_count,
          round(avg(arrayAvg(
              arrayMap((d1, d2) -> toInt32(dateDiff('day', d1, d2)),
                  arraySlice(arraySort(dates), 1, length(arraySort(dates)) - 1),
                  arraySlice(arraySort(dates), 2, length(arraySort(dates)) - 1)
              )
          )), 1)                           AS avg_interval_days
      FROM client_purchase_dates
      LIMIT 1

    SQL:
      
      SELECT
          p1.client_id,
          dateDiff('day', p1.date, p2.date) AS interval_days
      FROM dm_purchases p1
      INNER JOIN dm_purchases p2
          ON p1.client_id = p2.client_id
          AND p2.date > p1.date
          AND p2.date <= today()
      WHERE p1.date >= today() - INTERVAL 180 DAY
        AND p2.date >= today() - INTERVAL 180 DAY
        AND p1.city = 'Moscow'
        AND p1.client_id IN (
            SELECT buyers.client_id
            FROM (
                SELECT
                    client_id,
                    count()      AS purchase_count,
                    sum(revenue) AS total_revenue
                FROM dm_purchases
                WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 180 DAY
                  AND city = 'Moscow'
                GROUP BY client_id
                HAVING purchase_count >= 2
                  AND total_revenue / purchase_count > 15000
            ) buyers
            INNER JOIN dm_client_profile cp ON cp.client_id = buyers.client_id
            WHERE cp.last_device = '1'
        )
      LIMIT 100000

  📦 TOOL_RESULT  [clickhouse_query]  ~91 tok
    ✅ 559 rows | columns: client_id, interval_days

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [python_analysis]  ~593 tok
    CODE:
      
      # Анализ интервалов между покупками
      # Фильтруем только минимальные интервалы между соседними покупками (self-join даёт все пары)
      # Для честного "среднего интервала" берём только следующую покупку (минимальный будущий интервал)
      
      df_intervals = df.copy()
      
      # Берём минимальный интервал для каждой пары client_id (ближайшая следующая покупка)
      min_intervals = df_intervals.groupby('client_id')['interval_days'].min().reset_index()
      min_intervals.columns = ['client_id', 'next_interval_days']
      
      avg_interval = min_intervals['next_interval_days'].mean()
      median_interval = min_intervals['next_interval_days'].median()
      min_val = min_intervals['next_interval_days'].min()
      max_val = min_intervals['next_interval_days'].max()
      n_clients = min_intervals['client_id'].nunique()
      
      print(f"Клиентов: {n_clients}")
      print(f"Среднее: {avg_interval:.1f} дней")
      print(f"Медиана: {median_interval:.1f} дней")
      print(f"Мин: {min_val}, Макс: {max_val}")
      
      # Распределение по бакетам
      bins = [0, 7, 14, 30, 60, 90, 180]
      labels = ['1–7д', '8–14д', '15–30д', '31–60д', '61–90д', '91–180д']
      min_intervals['bucket'] = pd.cut(min_intervals['next_interval_days'], bins=bins, labels=labels)
      dist = min_intervals['bucket'].value_counts().reindex(labels)
      
      print("\nРаспределение:")
      print(dist)
      
      # Визуализация
      fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(8, 4))
      colors = ['#4e79a7' if v == dist.max() else '#a0c4e8' for v in dist.values]
      ax.bar(dist.index, dist.values, color=colors)
      ax.set_title('Интервал до следующей покупки — сегмент hv_desktop_moscow', fontsize=12)
      ax.set_xlabel('Интервал')
      ax.set_ylabel('Кол-во клиентов')
      for i, v in enumerate(dist.values):
          ax.text(i, v + 0.3, str(v), ha='center', fontsize=10)
      plt.tight_layout()
      plt.savefig('intervals.png')
      plt.show()
      
      result = f"""## Интервалы между покупками — hv_desktop_moscow
      
      | Метрика | Значение |
      |---|---|
      | Клиентов в сегменте | {n_clients:,} |
      | Средний интервал | **{avg_interval:.1f} дней** |
      | Медианный интервал | **{median_interval:.1f} дней** |
      | Минимальный | {min_val} дн. |
      | Максимальный | {max_val} дн. |
      
      **Распределение по интервалам:**
      
      | Интервал | Клиентов |
      |---|---|
      """ + "\n".join([f"| {label} | {val} |" for label, val in zip(labels, dist.values)])

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [python_analysis]  ~227 tok

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [clickhouse_query]  ~228 tok
    SQL:
      
      WITH segment AS (
          SELECT DISTINCT buyers.client_id
          FROM (
              SELECT
                  client_id,
                  count()        AS purchase_count,
                  sum(revenue)   AS total_revenue
              FROM dm_purchases
              WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 180 DAY
                AND city = 'Moscow'
              GROUP BY client_id
              HAVING purchase_count >= 2
                 AND total_revenue / purchase_count > 15000
          ) buyers
          INNER JOIN dm_client_profile cp ON cp.client_id = buyers.client_id
          WHERE cp.last_device = '1'
      )
      SELECT
          cp.first_utm_source,
          cj.utm_campaign,
          count(DISTINCT cj.client_id) AS clients
      FROM dm_client_journey cj
      INNER JOIN segment s ON s.client_id = cj.client_id
      INNER JOIN dm_client_profile cp ON cp.client_id = cj.client_id
      WHERE cj.visit_number = 1
      GROUP BY cp.first_utm_source, cj.utm_campaign
      ORDER BY clients DESC
      LIMIT 100

    CODE:
      
      total = df['clients'].sum()
      
      df['source_label'] = df['first_utm_source'].apply(
          lambda v: v if pd.notna(v) and str(v).strip() else '(direct / none)'
      )
      df['campaign_label'] = df['utm_campaign'].apply(
          lambda v: v if pd.notna(v) and str(v).strip() else '(нет кампании)'
      )
      df['pct'] = df['clients'] / total * 100
      
      # Группировка по source
      by_source = df.groupby('source_label')['clients'].sum().reset_index()
      by_source['pct'] = by_source['clients'] / total * 100
      by_source = by_source.sort_values('clients', ascending=False)
      
      # Детальная таблица
      detail = df[['source_label', 'campaign_label', 'clients', 'pct']].sort_values('clients', ascending=False)
      
      print(by_source.to_string())
      print()
      print(detail.to_string())
      
      # Формируем result
      rows_source = ""
      for _, r in by_source.iterrows():
          rows_source += f"| {r['source_label']} | {r['clients']:,} | {r['pct']:.1f}% |\n"
      
      rows_detail = ""
      for _, r in detail.iterrows():
          rows_detail += f"| {r['source_label']} | {r['campaign_label']} | {r['clients']:,} | {r['pct']:.1f}% |\n"
      
      result = f"""## Первое касание — hv_desktop_moscow ({total:,} клиентов)

      | utm_source | Клиентов | Доля |
      |---|---|---|
      {rows_source}
      ### По кампании (детально)
      
      | utm_source | utm_campaign | Клиентов | Доля |
      |---|---|---|---|
      {rows_detail}
      """

    SQL:
      
      SELECT
          converted,
          sources_path[1] AS first_touch_source,
          COUNT() AS users,
          ROUND(COUNT() * 100.0 / SUM(COUNT()) OVER (PARTITION BY converted), 2) AS pct
      FROM dm_conversion_paths
      WHERE length(sources_path) >= 2
        AND sources_path[2] = 'gdeslon'
      GROUP BY converted, first_touch_source
      ORDER BY converted DESC, users DESC
      LIMIT 30

  📦 TOOL_RESULT  [clickhouse_query]  ~128 tok
    ✅ 9 rows | columns: converted, first_touch_source, users, pct

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [python_analysis]  ~241 tok
    CODE:
      
      df['converted_label'] = df['converted'].map({1: 'Купили', 0: 'Не купили'})
      df['first_touch_source'] = df['first_touch_source'].replace('', '(не определён)')
      
      for segment, group in df.groupby('converted_label', sort=False):
          total = group['users'].sum()
          print(f"\n### {segment} — всего: {total:,}")
          print(group[['first_touch_source', 'users', 'pct']].to_string(index=False))
      
      result = ""
      for segment in ['Купили', 'Не купили']:
          group = df[df['converted_label'] == segment].sort_values('users', ascending=False)
          total = group['users'].sum()
          result += f"\n### {segment} (всего: {total:,})\n"
          result += "| # | Первый канал | Пользователей | % |\n|---|---|---:|---:|\n"
          for i, row in enumerate(group.itertuples(), 1):
              result += f"| {i} | {row.first_touch_source} | {row.users:,} | {row.pct}% |\n"

    а теперь рассмотрим топ 10 каналов для 3 визита. Если второй уже был

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [clickhouse_query]  ~101 tok
    SQL:
      
      SELECT
          converted,
          sources_path[3] AS third_touch_source,
          COUNT() AS users,
          ROUND(COUNT() * 100.0 / SUM(COUNT()) OVER (PARTITION BY converted), 1) AS pct
      FROM dm_conversion_paths
      WHERE length(sources_path) >= 3
        AND sources_path[2] != ''  -- второй визит неорганический (есть UTM)
      GROUP BY converted, third_touch_source
      ORDER BY converted DESC, users DESC
      LIMIT 40

  📦 TOOL_RESULT  [clickhouse_query]  ~128 tok
    ✅ 15 rows | columns: converted, third_touch_source, users, pct

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [python_analysis]  ~314 tok
    CODE:
      
      bought = df[df['converted'] == 1].sort_values('users', ascending=False).head(10)
      not_bought = df[df['converted'] == 0].sort_values('users', ascending=False).head(10)
      
      def label(v):
          return '(не определён)' if str(v).strip() == '' else str(v)
      
      bought['third_touch_source'] = bought['third_touch_source'].apply(label)
      not_bought['third_touch_source'] = not_bought['third_touch_source'].apply(label)
      
      total_bought = bought['users'].sum()
      total_not_bought = not_bought['users'].sum()
      
      rows_b = ""
      for i, row in enumerate(bought.itertuples(), 1):
          rows_b += f"| {i} | {row.third_touch_source} | {row.users:,} | {row.pct:.1f}% |\n"
      
      rows_nb = ""
      for i, row in enumerate(not_bought.itertuples(), 1):
          rows_nb += f"| {i} | {row.third_touch_source} | {row.users:,} | {row.pct:.1f}% |\n"
      
      result = f"""## Третье касание (второй визит был с UTM)
      
      ### Купили ({total_bought:,} человек)
      | # | Канал | Пользователей | % |
      |---|---|---:|---:|
      {rows_b}
      ### Не купили ({total_not_bought:,} человек)
      | # | Канал | Пользователей | % |
      |---|---|---:|---:|
      {rows_nb}
      """
      
      print(df.groupby('converted')['users'].sum())

    SQL:
      
      SELECT
          sources_path[3] AS third_touch_source,
          countIf(converted = 1) AS buyers,
          countIf(converted = 0) AS non_buyers,
          COUNT() AS total,
          SUM(revenue) AS revenue,
          ROUND(countIf(converted = 1) * 100.0 / COUNT(), 2) AS cr_pct,
          ROUND(SUM(revenue) / countIf(converted = 1), 0) AS avg_order
      FROM dm_conversion_paths
      WHERE length(sources_path) >= 3
        AND sources_path[2] != ''
      GROUP BY third_touch_source
      HAVING total >= 5
      ORDER BY buyers DESC
      LIMIT 10

    CODE:
      
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      
      print("Строк:", len(df))
      
      # Устройства
      device_map = {'1': 'Десктоп', '2': 'Мобильный', '3': 'Планшет', '4': 'TV'}
      df['device_label'] = df['last_device'].astype(str).map(device_map).fillna('Неизвестно')
      
      device_dist = df['device_label'].value_counts(normalize=True).mul(100).round(1)
      
      # Города — топ-10
      city_dist = df['last_city'].replace('', 'Не определён').value_counts().head(10)
      
      # Конверсия
      total = len(df)
      buyers = df['has_purchased'].sum()
      cr = buyers / total * 100
      
      # Визиты
      visits_median = df['total_visits'].median()
      visits_mean = df['total_visits'].mean()
      
      # Поисковик
      search_dist = df['last_search_engine'].replace('', 'Не определён').value_counts(normalize=True).mul(100).round(1)
      
      # Pageviews
      pv_median = df['total_pageviews'].median()
      pv_mean = df['total_pageviews'].mean()
      
      # Bounce rate
      df['bounce_rate'] = df['total_bounces'] / df['total_visits'].replace(0, np.nan)
      bounce_median = df['bounce_rate'].median()
      
      # Days since last visit
      days_median = df['days_since_last_visit'].median()
      days_mean = df['days_since_last_visit'].mean()
      
      # Покупатели vs нет
      buyers_df = df[df['has_purchased'] == 1]
      non_buyers_df = df[df['has_purchased'] == 0]
      
      print("Покупателей:", len(buyers_df), "Не купили:", len(non_buyers_df))
      print("\nУстройства:\n", device_dist)
      print("\nПоисковики:\n", search_dist)
      print("\nВизиты median/mean:", visits_median, visits_mean)
      print("\nPageviews median:", pv_median)
      print("\nDays since last visit median:", days_median)
      
      result = f"""## Аудитория: органика → Smart_bannery Retargeting
      
      **Выборка:** {total:,} пользователей | **Купили:** {int(buyers):,} ({cr:.1f}%)
      
      ### Устройства
      | Устройство | % |
      |---|---:|
      """ + "\n".join([f"| {k} | {v}% |" for k, v in device_dist.items()]) + f"""
      
      ### Поисковик первого визита
      | Поисковик | % |
      |---|---:|
      """ + "\n".join([f"| {k} | {v}% |" for k, v in search_dist.items()]) + f"""
      
      ### Поведенческий портрет
      | Метрика | Медиана | Среднее |
      |---|---:|---:|
      | Визитов на клиента | {visits_median:.0f} | {visits_mean:.1f} |
      | Просмотров страниц | {pv_median:.0f} | {pv_mean:.1f} |
      | Bounce rate | {bounce_median:.1%} | — |
      | Дней с последнего визита | {days_median:.0f} | {days_mean:.1f} |
      
      ### Топ-10 городов

    **Давно ушедшие** — медиана 121 день с последнего визита. Это не «горячий»
    ретаргетинг последних дней, а работа с давно ушедшей аудиторией. CR 2.1% —
    ожидаемо низкий для такого «холодного» сегмента.  ⚠️ Конверсия 2.1% при 121
    дне с последнего визита — сигнал, что окно ретаргетинга слишком широкое.
    Аудитория «перегорела».  Следующий шаг: сравнить CR этого сегмента с теми,
    кто вернулся в первые 7/14/30 дней — найти оптимальное окно ретаргетинга.

    Сделай анализ ya-direct за последние 3 месяца: найди кампании с аномалиями в
    CR по неделям (резкие всплески или падения). Для этих кампаний проверь
    когорту — клиенты которые пришли в период аномалии, какой у них retention за
    30 дней по сравнению с нормальным периодом?

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [clickhouse_query]  ~88 tok
    SQL:
      
      SELECT
          toStartOfWeek(date, 1) AS week,
          utm_campaign,
          SUM(visits) AS visits,
          SUM(sessions_with_purchase) AS purchases,
          SUM(revenue) AS revenue
      FROM dm_traffic_performance
      WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 3 MONTH
        AND utm_source = 'ya-direct'
      GROUP BY week, utm_campaign
      ORDER BY utm_campaign, week
      LIMIT 50000

    CODE:
      
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      import seaborn as sns
      
      df['week'] = pd.to_datetime(df['week'])
      df['cr'] = df['purchases'] / df['visits'].replace(0, np.nan)
      
      # Считаем baseline и z-score для каждой кампании
      results = []
      anomaly_campaigns = {}
      
      for campaign, grp in df.groupby('utm_campaign'):
          grp = grp.sort_values('week').copy()
          # Фильтрация: минимум 4 недели с визитами, мин 10 визитов в неделю
          grp_valid = grp[grp['visits'] >= 10].copy()
          if len(grp_valid) < 4:
              continue
          
          mean_cr = grp_valid['cr'].mean()
          std_cr = grp_valid['cr'].std()
          
          if std_cr == 0 or pd.isna(std_cr):
              continue
          
          grp_valid['z_score'] = (grp_valid['cr'] - mean_cr) / std_cr
          grp_valid['mean_cr'] = mean_cr
          grp_valid['std_cr'] = std_cr
          
          anomalies = grp_valid[grp_valid['z_score'].abs() > 2.0]
          
          if len(anomalies) > 0:
              anomaly_campaigns[campaign] = {
                  'data': grp_valid,
                  'anomalies': anomalies,
                  'mean_cr': mean_cr,
                  'std_cr': std_cr
              }
          
          for _, row in grp_valid.iterrows():
              results.append({
                  'campaign': campaign,
                  'week': row['week'],
                  'visits': row['visits'],
                  'purchases': row['purchases'],
                  'cr': row['cr'],
                  'z_score': row.get('z_score', np.nan),
                  'mean_cr': mean_cr,
                  'std_cr': std_cr
              })
      
      print(f"Кампаний с аномалиями: {len(anomaly_campaigns)}")
      for camp, info in anomaly_campaigns.items():
          print(f"\n  [{camp}]")
          print(f"  baseline CR: {info['mean_cr']:.2%} ± {info['std_cr']:.2%}")
          for _, a in info['anomalies'].iterrows():
              direction = "РОСТ" if a['z_score'] > 0 else "ПАДЕНИЕ"
              print(f"  {direction} неделя {a['week'].date()}: CR={a['cr']:.2%}, z={a['z_score']:.1f}σ, визитов={a['visits']}, покупок={a['purchases']}")

              'anomaly_type': 'РОСТ',
              'z': 2.8
          },
          'Poisk_|_Italyanskie_brendy_|_Moskva_i_obl': {
              'anomaly_weeks': ['2026-02-16'],

              'z': 2.0

              'z': 2.0
          },
      }

          ax.axhline(mean_cr * 100, color='gray', linestyle='--', alpha=0.7, label=f'Среднее {mean_cr:.2%}')
          ax.axhline((mean_cr + 2 * grp['cr'].std()) * 100, color='red', linestyle=':', alpha=0.5, label='+2σ')
          ax.axhline((mean_cr - 2 * grp['cr'].std()) * 100, color='orange', linestyle=':', alpha=0.5, label='-2σ')
      
          # Отметить аномальные недели
          for aw in info['anomaly_weeks']:
              aw_dt = pd.to_datetime(aw)
              anom_rows = grp[grp['week'] == aw_dt]
              if not anom_rows.empty:
                  ax.scatter(anom_rows['week'], anom_rows['cr'] * 100,
                             color='red', zorder=5, s=80, label=f'Аномалия ({info["z"]:.1f}σ)')
      
          short_name = camp.replace('Poisk_|_', '').replace('Smart_bannery_|_', 'SmB_').replace('_|_Moskva_i_obl', '').replace('_', ' ')
          ax.set_title(short_name, fontsize=10)
          ax.set_xlabel('Неделя', fontsize=8)
          ax.set_ylabel('CR, %', fontsize=8)
          ax.legend(fontsize=7)
          ax.tick_params(axis='x', rotation=45, labelsize=7)
      
      # Убрать лишний subplot
      axes[-1].set_visible(False)
      
      plt.suptitle('Аномалии CR по кампаниям ya-direct (последние 3 месяца)', fontsize=14, y=1.01)
      plt.tight_layout()
      
      # Итоговая таблица аномалий
      rows = []
      for camp, info in anomaly_campaigns_info.items():
          grp = df[df['utm_campaign'] == camp].copy()
          grp = grp[grp['visits'] >= 10]
          mean_cr = grp['cr'].mean()
          std_cr = grp['cr'].std()

              anom = grp[grp['week'] == aw_dt]
              if not anom.empty:

                      'CR норма': f"{mean_cr:.2%}",
                      'Z-score': f"{info['z']:.1f}σ",
                      'Визитов': int(r['visits']),
                      'Покупок': int(r['purchases'])
                  })
      
      anom_df = pd.DataFrame(rows)
      print(anom_df.to_string(index=False))

    CODE:
      
      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      
      df['week'] = pd.to_datetime(df['week'])
      df['cr'] = df['purchases'] / df['visits'].replace(0, np.nan)
      
      # Посмотрим на весь масштаб: сколько трафика и покупок по кампаниям
      summary = df.groupby('utm_campaign').agg(
          total_visits=('visits', 'sum'),
          total_purchases=('purchases', 'sum'),
          weeks_count=('week', 'nunique'),
          avg_weekly_visits=('visits', 'mean'),
          avg_weekly_purchases=('purchases', 'mean'),
          total_revenue=('revenue', 'sum')
      ).sort_values('total_visits', ascending=False)
      
      summary['avg_cr'] = summary['total_purchases'] / summary['total_visits']
      summary = summary.reset_index()
      
      print("=== Все кампании ya-direct: масштаб ===")
      print(summary[['utm_campaign', 'total_visits', 'total_purchases', 'avg_cr', 'weeks_count', 'avg_weekly_purchases']].to_string(index=False))
      
      # Кампании с достаточным трафиком для надёжного CR-анализа (>=50 покупок за 3 мес)
      reliable = summary[summary['total_purchases'] >= 10].copy()
      print(f"\nКампаний с >=10 покупками за 3 мес: {len(reliable)}")
      print(reliable[['utm_campaign', 'total_visits', 'total_purchases', 'avg_cr']].to_string(index=False))
      
      result = "done"

      import pandas as pd
      import numpy as np
      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      
      df['week'] = pd.to_datetime(df['week'])
      df['cr'] = df['purchases'] / df['visits'].replace(0, np.nan)
      
      # Только кампании с >=10 покупками
      reliable_camps = [
          'mk_okt23|98230218',
          'Smart_bannery_|_Retargeting_|_Moskva_i_MO_new|97370670',
          'Poisk_|_Tovarnaya_galereya_|_Fid_|_Moskva_i_obl',
          'Poisk_|_Brend_|_Moskva_i_oblast',
          'Smart_bannery_|_Detskie_unitazy_|_Moskva_i_obl'
      ]
      
      df_rel = df[df['utm_campaign'].isin(reliable_camps)].copy()
      
      # Z-score для каждой кампании
      anomaly_list = []
      camp_stats = {}
      
      for camp, grp in df_rel.groupby('utm_campaign'):
          grp = grp[grp['visits'] >= 10].sort_values('week').copy()
          if len(grp) < 4:
              continue
          mean_cr = grp['cr'].mean()
          std_cr = grp['cr'].std()
          camp_stats[camp] = {'mean_cr': mean_cr, 'std_cr': std_cr, 'data': grp}
          if std_cr == 0:
              continue
          grp['z_score'] = (grp['cr'] - mean_cr) / std_cr
          anom = grp[grp['z_score'].abs() > 1.7].copy()  # чуть мягче порог
          for _, row in anom.iterrows():
              anomaly_list.append({
                  'utm_campaign': camp,
                  'week': row['week'],
                  'cr': row['cr'],
                  'mean_cr': mean_cr,
                  'z_score': row['z_score'],
                  'visits': row['visits'],
                  'purchases': int(row['purchases']),
                  'revenue': row['revenue']
              })
      
      anom_df = pd.DataFrame(anomaly_list)
      print(f"Аномальных недель (z > 1.7): {len(anom_df)}")
      print(anom_df[['utm_campaign', 'week', 'cr', 'mean_cr', 'z_score', 'visits', 'purchases']].to_string(index=False))
      
      # --- График ---
      fig, axes = plt.subplots(3, 2, figsize=(16, 14))
      axes = axes.flatten()
      
      labels = {
          'mk_okt23|98230218': 'mk_okt23 (основная)',
          'Smart_bannery_|_Retargeting_|_Moskva_i_MO_new|97370670': 'Смарт-баннеры Ретаргетинг',
          'Poisk_|_Tovarnaya_galereya_|_Fid_|_Moskva_i_obl': 'Поиск Товарная галерея',
          'Poisk_|_Brend_|_Moskva_i_oblast': 'Поиск Бренд',
          'Smart_bannery_|_Detskie_unitazy_|_Moskva_i_obl': 'Смарт-баннеры Детские унитазы'
      }
      
      for idx, (camp, stats) in enumerate(camp_stats.items()):
          ax = axes[idx]
          grp = stats['data'].sort_values('week')
          mean_cr = stats['mean_cr']
          std_cr = stats['std_cr']
          
          ax.plot(grp['week'], grp['cr'] * 100, marker='o', color='steelblue', linewidth=2, markersize=5, label='CR, %')
          ax.axhline(mean_cr * 100, color='gray', linestyle='--', alpha=0.8, linewidth=1.5, label=f'Среднее {mean_cr:.2%}')
          ax.axhline((mean_cr + 1.7 * std_cr) * 100, color='red', linestyle=':', alpha=0.6, label='+1.7σ')
          ax.axhline(max(0, mean_cr - 1.7 * std_cr) * 100, color='orange', linestyle=':', alpha=0.6, label='-1.7σ')
          
          # Аномальные точки
          anom_weeks = anom_df[anom_df['utm_campaign'] == camp]['week']
          for aw in anom_weeks:
              apts = grp[grp['week'] == aw]
              if not apts.empty:
                  color = 'red' if apts.iloc[0]['z_score'] > 0 else 'darkorange'
                  ax.scatter(apts['week'], apts['cr'] * 100, color=color, zorder=5, s=100)
          
          ax.set_title(labels.get(camp, camp), fontsize=10)
          ax.set_xlabel('Неделя', fontsize=8)
          ax.set_ylabel('CR, %', fontsize=8)
          ax.legend(fontsize=7, loc='upper right')
          ax.tick_params(axis='x', rotation=45, labelsize=7)
      
      axes[-1].set_visible(False)
      plt.suptitle('Недельный CR по кампаниям ya-direct — аномалии', fontsize=14, y=1.01)
      plt.tight_layout()
      
      result = "charts_ready"

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [clickhouse_query]  ~588 tok
    SQL:
      
      -- Клиенты из аномальных и нормальных периодов двух кампаний
      -- Товарная галерея: аномалия 12–18 января 2026, норма = остальные недели
      -- Детские унитазы: аномалия 8–14 декабря 2025, норма = остальные недели
      WITH anomaly_clients AS (
          SELECT DISTINCT
              client_id,
              utm_campaign,
              date,
              CASE
                  WHEN utm_campaign = 'Poisk_|_Tovarnaya_galereya_|_Fid_|_Moskva_i_obl'
                       AND date >= '2026-01-12' AND date <= '2026-01-18' THEN 'anomaly'
                  WHEN utm_campaign = 'Smart_bannery_|_Detskie_unitazy_|_Moskva_i_obl'
                       AND date >= '2025-12-08' AND date <= '2025-12-14' THEN 'anomaly'
                  ELSE 'normal'
              END AS period_type
          FROM dm_client_journey
          WHERE utm_source = 'ya-direct'
            AND utm_campaign IN (
                'Poisk_|_Tovarnaya_galereya_|_Fid_|_Moskva_i_obl',
                'Smart_bannery_|_Detskie_unitazy_|_Moskva_i_obl'
            )
            AND date >= today() - INTERVAL 3 MONTH
      ),
      -- Первый визит каждого клиента в кампании (дата входа в когорту)
      first_visit AS (
          SELECT
              client_id,
              utm_campaign,
              period_type,
              MIN(date) AS cohort_date
          FROM anomaly_clients
          GROUP BY client_id, utm_campaign, period_type
      ),
      -- Был ли клиент активен в течение 30 дней после первого визита
      return_visit AS (
          SELECT
              fv.client_id,
              fv.utm_campaign,
              fv.period_type,
              fv.cohort_date,
              MAX(CASE WHEN j.date > fv.cohort_date AND j.date <= fv.cohort_date + INTERVAL 30 DAY THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS returned_30d,
              MAX(CASE WHEN j.has_purchase = 1 AND j.date > fv.cohort_date AND j.date <= fv.cohort_date + INTERVAL 30 DAY THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS purchased_30d
          FROM first_visit fv
          LEFT JOIN dm_client_journey j ON fv.client_id = j.client_id
          GROUP BY fv.client_id, fv.utm_campaign, fv.period_type, fv.cohort_date
      )
      SELECT
          utm_campaign,
          period_type,
          COUNT(DISTINCT client_id) AS cohort_size,
          SUM(returned_30d) AS returned_count,
          SUM(purchased_30d) AS purchased_count,
          SUM(returned_30d) / COUNT(DISTINCT client_id) AS retention_30d,
          SUM(purchased_30d) / COUNT(DISTINCT client_id) AS repeat_purchase_rate
      FROM return_visit
      GROUP BY utm_campaign, period_type
      ORDER BY utm_campaign, period_type
      LIMIT 100

  🤔 THINKING  ~77 tok
    ⚠️ Честная диагностика перед переходом к retention: все 3 аномалии имеют
    **3–4 покупки** в пике. Это малые числа — статистически значимая аномалия
    только условно. Тем не менее, разберём retention для двух «роств» (Товарная
    галерея 2026-01-12 и Детские унитазы 2025-12-08) vs нормальные недели тех же
    кампаний.

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [clickhouse_query]  ~462 tok
    SQL:
      
      WITH first_visit AS (
          SELECT
              client_id,
              utm_campaign,
              MIN(date) AS cohort_date,
              CASE
                  WHEN utm_campaign = 'Poisk_|_Tovarnaya_galereya_|_Fid_|_Moskva_i_obl'
                       AND MIN(date) >= '2026-01-12' AND MIN(date) <= '2026-01-18' THEN 'anomaly'
                  WHEN utm_campaign = 'Smart_bannery_|_Detskie_unitazy_|_Moskva_i_obl'
                       AND MIN(date) >= '2025-12-08' AND MIN(date) <= '2025-12-14' THEN 'anomaly'
                  ELSE 'normal'
              END AS period_type
          FROM dm_client_journey
          WHERE utm_source = 'ya-direct'
            AND utm_campaign IN (
                'Poisk_|_Tovarnaya_galereya_|_Fid_|_Moskva_i_obl',
                'Smart_bannery_|_Detskie_unitazy_|_Moskva_i_obl'
            )
            AND date >= today() - INTERVAL 3 MONTH
          GROUP BY client_id, utm_campaign
      ),
      return_visit AS (
          SELECT
              fv.client_id,
              fv.utm_campaign,
              fv.period_type,
              fv.cohort_date,
              maxIf(1, j.date > fv.cohort_date AND j.date <= fv.cohort_date + INTERVAL 30 DAY) AS returned_30d,
              maxIf(1, j.has_purchase = 1 AND j.date > fv.cohort_date AND j.date <= fv.cohort_date + INTERVAL 30 DAY) AS purchased_30d
          FROM first_visit fv
          LEFT JOIN dm_client_journey j ON fv.client_id = j.client_id
          GROUP BY fv.client_id, fv.utm_campaign, fv.period_type, fv.cohort_date
      )
      SELECT
          utm_campaign,
          period_type,
          countDistinct(client_id) AS cohort_size,
          sum(returned_30d) AS returned_count,
          sum(purchased_30d) AS purchased_count,
          round(sum(returned_30d) / countDistinct(client_id) * 100, 1) AS retention_30d_pct,
          round(sum(purchased_30d) / countDistinct(client_id) * 100, 1) AS repeat_purchase_pct
      FROM return_visit
      GROUP BY utm_campaign, period_type
      ORDER BY utm_campaign, period_type
      LIMIT 100

    SQL:
      
      SELECT
          fv.utm_campaign,
          fv.period_type,
          count(DISTINCT fv.client_id) AS cohort_size,
          sum(fv.returned_30d) AS returned_count,
          sum(fv.purchased_30d) AS purchased_count,
          round(sum(fv.returned_30d) / count(DISTINCT fv.client_id) * 100, 1) AS retention_30d_pct,
          round(sum(fv.purchased_30d) / count(DISTINCT fv.client_id) * 100, 1) AS repeat_purchase_pct
      FROM (
          SELECT
              base.client_id,
              base.utm_campaign,
              base.cohort_date,
              base.period_type,
              maxIf(1, j2.date > base.cohort_date AND j2.date <= base.cohort_date + INTERVAL 30 DAY) AS returned_30d,
              maxIf(1, j2.has_purchase = 1 AND j2.date > base.cohort_date AND j2.date <= base.cohort_date + INTERVAL 30 DAY) AS purchased_30d
          FROM (
              SELECT
                  client_id,
                  utm_campaign,
                  min(date) AS cohort_date,
                  multiIf(
                      utm_campaign = 'Poisk_|_Tovarnaya_galereya_|_Fid_|_Moskva_i_obl' AND min(date) >= '2026-01-12' AND min(date) <= '2026-01-18', 'anomaly',
                      utm_campaign = 'Smart_bannery_|_Detskie_unitazy_|_Moskva_i_obl' AND min(date) >= '2025-12-08' AND min(date) <= '2025-12-14', 'anomaly',
                      'normal'
                  ) AS period_type
              FROM dm_client_journey
              WHERE utm_source = 'ya-direct'
                AND utm_campaign IN (
                    'Poisk_|_Tovarnaya_galereya_|_Fid_|_Moskva_i_obl',
                    'Smart_bannery_|_Detskie_unitazy_|_Moskva_i_obl'
                )
                AND date >= today() - INTERVAL 3 MONTH
              GROUP BY client_id, utm_campaign
          ) AS base
          LEFT JOIN dm_client_journey j2 ON base.client_id = j2.client_id
          GROUP BY base.client_id, base.utm_campaign, base.cohort_date, base.period_type
      ) AS fv
      GROUP BY fv.utm_campaign, fv.period_type
      ORDER BY fv.utm_campaign, fv.period_type
      LIMIT 100

          'Poisk_|_Tovarnaya_galereya_|_Fid_|_Moskva_i_obl': 'Поиск · Товарная галерея',
          'Smart_bannery_|_Detskie_unitazy_|_Moskva_i_obl': 'Смарт-баннеры · Детские унитазы'
      }

      ret_df['period_label'] = ret_df['period_type'].map({'anomaly': 'Аномалия', 'normal': 'Норма'})
      
      print(ret_df[['campaign_label', 'period_label', 'cohort_size', 'returned_count', 'purchased_count', 'retention_30d_pct', 'repeat_purchase_pct']].to_string(index=False))

      fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(14, 6))
      
      campaigns = ret_df['utm_campaign'].unique()
      colors = {'Аномалия': '#e74c3c', 'Норма': '#2980b9'}
      
      for ax_idx, camp in enumerate(campaigns):
          ax = axes[ax_idx]
          sub = ret_df[ret_df['utm_campaign'] == camp].sort_values('period_label')
          
          bars = ax.bar(
              sub['period_label'],
              sub['retention_30d_pct'],
              color=[colors[p] for p in sub['period_label']],
              width=0.5,
              edgecolor='white',
              linewidth=1.5
          )
          
          for bar, val, n in zip(bars, sub['retention_30d_pct'], sub['cohort_size']):
              ax.text(bar.get_x() + bar.get_width() / 2, bar.get_height() + 0.3,
                      f'{val:.1f}%\n(n={n:,})', ha='center', va='bottom', fontsize=11, fontweight='bold')
          
          ax.set_title(labels[camp], fontsize=11)
          ax.set_ylabel('Retention 30 дней, %', fontsize=10)
          ax.set_ylim(0, max(sub['retention_30d_pct']) * 1.35)
          ax.tick_params(axis='x', labelsize=11)
          ax.tick_params(axis='y', labelsize=9)
          ax.spines['top'].set_visible(False)
          ax.spines['right'].set_visible(False)

    ## Что я умею  Я аналитик рекламных данных, работающий прямо с вашей
    ClickHouse-базой. Вот что я делаю:  ---  ### Трафик и кампании - Сколько
    визитов, новых пользователей, отказов по
    источникам/кампаниям/устройствам/городам - Сравнение периодов: неделя к
    неделе, месяц к месяцу - Эффективность UTM-меток: source, medium, campaign,
    content  ### Конверсии и воронка - CR по каждому этапу: визит → сессия с
    покупкой → покупка - Где теряются пользователи, на каком канале хуже всего
    воронка - Bounce rate, глубина просмотра, длительность сессий  ### Покупки и
    revenue - Топ продуктов, категорий, городов по выручке - Средний чек,
    количество покупок, динамика по датам - Какой канал/кампания приносит
    деньги, а какой — только трафик  ### Клиентское поведение - Портрет клиента:
    откуда пришёл, сколько визитов до покупки, устройство, город - Повторные
    покупки, LTV, давность последнего визита - Сегментация: кто купил один раз,
    кто возвращается  ### Пути к конверсии - Какие цепочки каналов приводят к
    покупке - First touch vs last touch атрибуция - Длина пути, окно конверсии
    ### Drill-down и диагностика - Аномалии в данных: резкий рост/падение
    трафика, нулевые покупки у канала - Сравнение сегментов: мобайл vs десктоп,
    Москва vs регионы - Гипотезы и их проверка по данным  ---  ### Как работаю
    Пишу SQL-запросы в ClickHouse, анализирую в Python, строю графики — всё
    прямо здесь. Держу контекст сессии: если ты уже спросил про один канал,
    следующий вопрос понимаю как продолжение.  **Просто спроси** — я пойму,
    нужна ли цифра, таблица, график или разбор аномалии.

    SQL:
      
      SELECT 
          date,
          SUM(visits) AS visits,
          SUM(sessions_with_purchase) AS purchases,
          SUM(revenue) AS revenue
      FROM dm_traffic_performance
      WHERE date >= toStartOfMonth(today() - INTERVAL 1 MONTH) AND date < toStartOfMonth(today())
      GROUP BY date
      ORDER BY date

      import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
      import matplotlib.ticker as mticker
      import pandas as pd
      
      df['date'] = pd.to_datetime(df['date'])
      
      fig, (ax1, ax2, ax3) = plt.subplots(3, 1, figsize=(13, 10), sharex=True)
      fig.suptitle("Февраль 2026 — общая динамика", fontsize=15, fontweight='bold', y=0.98)
      
      # Визиты
      ax1.fill_between(df['date'], df['visits'], alpha=0.3, color='#4C72B0')
      ax1.plot(df['date'], df['visits'], color='#4C72B0', linewidth=2)
      ax1.set_ylabel("Визиты")
      ax1.yaxis.set_major_formatter(mticker.FuncFormatter(lambda x, _: f"{x:,.0f}"))
      ax1.set_title("Визиты", fontsize=11, loc='left')
      ax1.grid(axis='y', linestyle='--', alpha=0.5)
      
      # Покупки
      ax2.fill_between(df['date'], df['purchases'], alpha=0.3, color='#55A868')
      ax2.plot(df['date'], df['purchases'], color='#55A868', linewidth=2)
      ax2.set_ylabel("Покупки")
      ax2.yaxis.set_major_formatter(mticker.FuncFormatter(lambda x, _: f"{x:,.0f}"))
      ax2.set_title("Сессии с покупкой", fontsize=11, loc='left')
      ax2.grid(axis='y', linestyle='--', alpha=0.5)
      
      # Выручка
      ax3.fill_between(df['date'], df['revenue'], alpha=0.3, color='#C44E52')
      ax3.plot(df['date'], df['revenue'], color='#C44E52', linewidth=2)
      ax3.set_ylabel("Выручка, ₽")
      ax3.yaxis.set_major_formatter(mticker.FuncFormatter(lambda x, _: f"{x/1_000_000:.1f}M"))
      ax3.set_title("Выручка", fontsize=11, loc='left')
      ax3.grid(axis='y', linestyle='--', alpha=0.5)
      ax3.set_xlabel("Дата")
      
      import matplotlib.dates as mdates
      ax3.xaxis.set_major_formatter(mdates.DateFormatter('%d.%m'))
      ax3.xaxis.set_major_locator(mdates.DayLocator(interval=3))
      plt.xticks(rotation=30)
      
      plt.tight_layout()
      
      # Итоги в result
      total_visits = df['visits'].sum()
      total_purchases = df['purchases'].sum()
      total_revenue = df['revenue'].sum()
      avg_cr = total_purchases / total_visits * 100
      
      result = f"""## Февраль 2026 — итого
      
      | Метрика | Значение |
      |---|---|

      | Выручка | {total_revenue:,.0f} ₽ |
      """

      FROM visits
      WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 30 DAY
        AND clientID > 0

  🔧 TOOL_CALL  [clickhouse_query]  ~57 tok
    SQL:
      
      SELECT 
          count() AS total_purchases,
          count(DISTINCT client_id) AS unique_buyers,
          sum(revenue) AS total_revenue,
          avg(revenue) AS avg_check
      FROM dm_purchases
      WHERE date >= today() - INTERVAL 30 DAY
